Exxon,2017-9,"UPDATE 3-BP-led group extends Azeri oil ""contract of the century"" - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170914T155402.127+0000}}UPDATE 3-BP-led group extends Azeri oil ""contract of the century""* Deal to extend ACG field development into 2050"
Exxon,2017-9,"BAKU/LONDON, Sept 14 (Reuters) - BP and Azerbaijan agreed on Thursday to extend into 2050 a contract to develop the ex-Soviet state's biggest oilfield cluster, a deal dubbed ""the contract of the century"" when first signed in 1994."
Exxon,2017-9,"Under the new production sharing agreement, the Azeri state energy company SOCAR will increase its share to 25 percent from 11.65 percent, while BP's stake declines to 30.37 percent from 35.8 percent. BP will remain the operator."
Exxon,2017-9,"The new contract secures large investment in Azerbaijan's oil sector for decades and a one-off bonus of $3.6 billion for the government, a welcome boost to a nation that has struggled with a sharp drop in oil prices in the past three years."
Exxon,2017-9,"""This bonus will be paid to Azerbaijan in eight tranches in the next eight years after an agreement is ratified by Azerbaijan's parliament,"" a source at SOCAR told Reuters."
Exxon,2017-9,The 1994 agreement to develop the giant Azeri-Chirag-Guneshli (ACG) fields in the Caspian Sea was transformative for Baku's political and economic development after the collapse of the Soviet Union.
Exxon,2017-9,"The new deal, whose exact terms were not disclosed, remains profitable for its partners at current oil prices of $55 a barrel, BP Chief Executive Officer Bob Dudley said in an interview. [nL5N1LV41H]"
Exxon,2017-9,"The fields produce 585,000 barrels per day, accounting for three quarters of the Azerbaijan's oil output, but production is expected to rise as the partners could invest up to $40 billion in the next 32 years, according to a statement."
Exxon,2017-9,"""There are still billions of barrels to recover and billions of dollars to invest"" in the project, said Wood Mackenzie analyst Laura Bennie."
Exxon,2017-9,"""Attention will now turn to a brand-new production platform (Azeri Central East), which will be commissioned in the 2020s,"" she said."
Exxon,2017-9,Azeri President Ilham Aliyev said the remaining oil reserves of the ACG oilfields stood at 500 million tonnes.
Exxon,2017-9,"Stakes of other firms in the consortium have also been reduced. Chevron now has 9.57 percent, Inpex <1605.T> 9.31 percent, Statoil 7.27 percent, ExxonMobil 6.79 percent, TPAO 5.73 percent, Itochu <8001.T> 3.65 percent and ONGC Videsh 2.31 percent."
Exxon,2017-9,"UPDATE 1-Kashagan to cut CPC oil supplies to 700,000 tonnes in Sept - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170914T152039.895+0000}}UPDATE 1-Kashagan to cut CPC oil supplies to 700,000 tonnes in Sept(Adds details)"
Exxon,2017-9,"MOSCOW, Sept 14 (Reuters) - Kazakhstan's giant Kashagan oil field will feed about 700,000 tonnes of oil into the CPC pipeline this month, 400,000 tonnes less than originally planned, a CPC official told Reuters on Thursday."
Exxon,2017-9,"Kashagan shipments via CPC have fallen below 10,000 tonnes per day this month after holding near 25,000 for several months, according to two sources familiar with the matter."
Exxon,2017-9,The two sources said Kashagan - which is an offshore field - had cut supplies because of some deposits being flooded by water. A third source said the field's processing plant had suffered a power outage last week.
Exxon,2017-9,"The sources said Kashagan's daily output was now approaching normal levels, but the issue has not been resolved completely."
Exxon,2017-9,"North Caspian Operating Company (NCOC), which operates Kashagan, did not reply to questions from Reuters about the reduction."
Exxon,2017-9,"NCOC includes Eni , Total , Shell , ExxonMobil , Kazakh state firm KazMunayGaz, China's CNPC and Japan's Inpex <1605.T>."

Exxon,2017-9,"HOUSTON, Sept 13 (Reuters) - ExxonMobil Corp may return its 362,300 barrel per day (bpd) Beaumont, Texas, refinery to full production by the end of September, said sources familiar with plant operations on Wednesday."
Exxon,2017-9,Exxon spokeswoman Charlotte Huffaker said the company did not have a timeline for resuming normal operations at the Beaumont refinery.
Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon was initiating the refinery's restart on Wednesday, Huffaker said. The refinery was shut on Aug. 30 when Tropical Storm Harvey inundated the Beaumont area."
Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon was warming up the Beaumont refinery's small crude distillation unit (CDU) on Wednesday ahead of the restart, the sources said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Energy industry intelligence service Genscape said on Wednesday its cameras observed increased activity at the 110,000-bpd Crude A CDU."
Exxon,2017-9,CDUs do the initial refining of crude oil coming into a refinery and provide feedstock for all other productions units.
Exxon,2017-9,Exxon spokeswoman Charlotte Huffaker said the company did not have a timeline for resuming normal operations at the Beaumont refinery.
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170913T225633.573+0000}}UPDATE 1-Exxon restarting Beaumont, Texas, refinery (Updates with Exxon statement)"
Exxon,2017-9,"HOUSTON, Sept 13 (Reuters) - ExxonMobil Corp said on Wednesday it was restarting the 362,300-barrel-per-day Beaumont, Texas, refinery for the first time since it was shut by Tropical Storm Harvey."
Exxon,2017-9,"""We are initiating restart of the Beaumont refinery,"" said Exxon spokeswoman Charlotte Huffaker."
Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon was warming up the Beaumont refinery's small crude distillation unit (CDU) for restart on Wednesday, said sources familiar with plant operations."
Exxon,2017-9,"Energy industry intelligence service Genscape said on Wednesday its cameras observed increased activity at the 110,000-bpd Crude A CDU."
Exxon,2017-9,The refinery was shut on Aug. 30 as Storm Harvey inundated the Beaumont area.
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170913T223555.849+0000}}BRIEF-Exxon says initiating restart of Beaumont, Texas refinerySept 13 (Reuters) - ExxonMobil Corp :"
Exxon,2017-9,Related: ExxonMobil Corp was preparing on Wednesday the small crude distillation unit (CDU) for restart at Beaumont refinery - sources [nL2N1LU293]
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170913T220336.831+0000}}Exxon Beaumont refinery preparing small CDU for restart -sourcesHOUSTON, Sept 13 (Reuters) - ExxonMobil Corp was preparing on Wednesday the small crude distillation unit (CDU) for restart at its shut 362,300 barrel per day (bpd) Beaumont, Texas, refinery, said sources familiar with plant operations."
Exxon,2017-9,"Energy industry intelligence service Genscape said on Wednesday its cameras observed increased activity at the 110,000 bpd Crude A CDU. The sources said Exxon was warming up the unit to operational temperature ahead of resuming production for the first time since the refinery was shut on Aug. 30 by Hurricane Harvey."
Exxon,2017-9,UPDATE 1-Norway gas pipeline investors go to top court over tariff cut - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170913T154315.813+0000}}UPDATE 1-Norway gas pipeline investors go to top court over tariff cut(Adds detail, background)"
Exxon,2017-9,"OSLO, Sept 13 (Reuters) - A group of investors in Norway's gas pipeline network are going to the country's highest court in a final attempt to overturn a government decision to cut pipeline tariffs that came into effect in October 2016."
Exxon,2017-9,"The Supreme Court is expected to decide whether to hear the case in late 2017, one of the investors, Solveig Gas, said in a statement. The hearing, if accepted, will take place in 2018."
Exxon,2017-9,"The government owns 45.8 percent of the Gassled pipeline network via state-owned Petoro, while majority state-owned Statoil has 5 percent."
Exxon,2017-9,"The four investors pursuing the case own a combined 43.9 percent stake. They are in turn owned by Allianz , UBS , the Abu Dhabi Investment Authority, Canada's Public Sector Pension Investment Board, the Canada Pension Plan Investment Board and France's Caisse des Depots."
Exxon,2017-9,"In June, a Norwegian appeals court ruled against the four in a lawsuit that argued the cut in gas pipeline tariffs was unlawful and would cost them a combined 15 billion Norwegian crowns ($1.8 billion) in lost earnings through 2028."
Exxon,2017-9,"That verdict overturned a previous decision, and awarded the government 42.2 million crowns from the plaintiffs."
Exxon,2017-9,Some of the companies involved have said the unexpected decision to lower gas transportation tariffs would hurt the image of Norway as a country to invest in.
Exxon,2017-9,"The government cut tariffs shortly after the four investors bought their stakes in Gassled in 2011 and 2012 from ExxonMobil , Total , Statoil and Royal Dutch Shell for a total of 32 billion crowns."
Exxon,2017-9,Norway's ministry of Petroleum and Energy was not immediately available for comment.
Exxon,2017-9,Gassled partners to appeal to Norwegian Supreme Court - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170913T142808.567+0000}}Gassled partners to appeal to Norwegian Supreme CourtOSLO, Sept 13 (Reuters) - Four partners in Gassled, Norway's gas infrastructure network, will appeal to the Norwegian Supreme Court a decision by a lower court that found in favour of the Norwegian state regarding the setting of network tariffs, two of the plaintiffs said on Wednesday."
Exxon,2017-9,"The Supreme Court is expected to decide whether to hear the case in late 2017, one of the partners, Solveig Gas, said in a statement."
Exxon,2017-9,RPT-UPDATE 1-Shell set to draw line under a century of Iraqi oil  - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170913T125245.478+0000}}RPT-UPDATE 1-Shell set to draw line under a century of Iraqi oil (Repeats to additional clients, no changes to text)"
Exxon,2017-9,"LONDON, Sept 13 (Reuters) - Royal Dutch Shell is set to end a century of oil production in Iraq by withdrawing from two of the Arab state's flagship fields to focus on more profitable gas development."
Exxon,2017-9,"Shell's retreat highlights the challenges foreign operators face with low-margin oil contracts in Iraq, an OPEC member that sits on some of the world's biggest oil reserves and wants to boost production after years of conflict hindered development."
Exxon,2017-9,The Anglo-Dutch firm said on Wednesday it had agreed with Iraq's oil ministry to relinquish operations at Majnoon field to the government after unfavourable changes to fiscal terms. The announcement confirmed an earlier Reuters report. [nL5N1LT67P]
Exxon,2017-9,Shell is also selling its 20 percent stake in West Qurna 1 oil field in the south of the country. The field is operated by Exxon Mobil .
Exxon,2017-9,"Investment bank Lazard is running the sale for Shell, industry sources told Reuters. The bank did not immediately respond to a request for comment. [nL5N1LU2JV]"
Exxon,2017-9,"Shell said it was still committed to producing gas in Iraq, saying it would focus on developing and expanding the Basra Gas Company, which processes gas from the Rumaila, West Qurna and Zubair fields. It has a 44 percent stake in the joint venture."
Exxon,2017-9,"Shell produced almost 20 million barrels of oil from Iraq during 2016, which accounted for about 3.5 percent of the firm's total oil output last year, according to Shell's annual report."
Exxon,2017-9,Precise terms of the contract terms are not public and Shell has not detailed its earnings from Iraqi oil.
Exxon,2017-9,"But a source told Reuters last year Shell had found limited financial benefit in recent years from oil production in Iraq, where it is paid in crude but has limited say on strategy. [nL8N1DT50R]"
Exxon,2017-9,"""The Oil Minister of Iraq formally endorsed a recent Shell proposal to pursue an amicable and mutually acceptable release of the Shell interest in Majnoon, with the timeline to be agreed in due course,"" a Shell company spokesman said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Shell took the decision after Iraq applied performance penalties on the Shell-operated venture ""which had a significant impact on its commerciality,"" he said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Battling a sharp fall in oil prices since 2014, Iraq asked foreign firms to cut spending on oil projects in order to reduce the cash-strapped government's contribution in shared ventures."
Exxon,2017-9,"Foreign firms in Iraq have long urged Baghdad to revise oil production contract terms to encourage development of reserves that Iraq estimates at about 153 billion barrels, the fourth biggest in the Organization of Petroleum Exporting Countries."
Exxon,2017-9,"""Maybe now they will speed things up,"" one executive from another company operating in Iraq said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Shell, via its subsidiary Anglo Saxon Oil Company, was among a consortium of European firms called Turkish Petroleum Company which acquired concessions in 1912 from the Ottoman Empire to explore for oil in today's Iraq. Oil was found 15 years later."
Exxon,2017-9,"Shell started developing Majnoon, which means ""crazy"" in Arabic, in 2010."
Exxon,2017-9,"It holds a 45 percent stake in the field that it operates under a technical service contract that expires in 2030. Malaysia's national oil company Petronas holds a 30 percent stake, while Iraqi government holds 25 percent."

Exxon,2017-9,Shell selling its stake in Iraq's West Qurna 1 oil field - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170913T101134.705+0000}}Shell selling its stake in Iraq's West Qurna 1 oil fieldLONDON, Sept 13 (Reuters) - Royal Dutch Shell is in the process of selling its 20 percent stake in Iraq's West Qurna 1 oil field, a spokesman said on Wednesday."
Exxon,2017-9,"The move comes as the Anglo-Dutch company said it had handed back to the Iraqi government operations at the Majnoon oil venture, one of the largest fields in OPEC member Iraq. [nL5N1LU0YY]"
Exxon,2017-9,"A spokesman for the company confirmed that Shell's stake in the West Qurna field, operated by Exxon Mobil , was subject to an ongoing sales process."
Exxon,2017-9,Exxon spokeswoman Charlotte Huffaker said the company did not have a timeline for resuming normal operations at the Beaumont refinery.

Exxon,2017-9,"UPDATE 2-U.S. Coast Guard, EPA cleaning up a dozen Texas chemical spills after Harvey - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170911T221931.717+0000}}UPDATE 2-U.S. Coast Guard, EPA cleaning up a dozen Texas chemical spills after Harvey(Adds NuStar comment in paragraph 8)"
Exxon,2017-9,"HOUSTON, Sept 11 (Reuters) - The U.S. Coast Guard and the Environmental Protection Agency are working with Texas state regulators to clean up oil and chemicals spilled from a dozen industrial facilities after flooding from Hurricane Harvey, authorities said."
Exxon,2017-9,"The spills came from oil refineries, fuel terminals and other businesses, but EPA spokeswoman Terri White said it was not possible to provide an estimate for the amounts spilled."
Exxon,2017-9,"""Initial reports were based on observation,"" White said. ""Some spills were already being cleaned up by the time EPA or other officials arrived to assess them and others had already migrated offsite."""
Exxon,2017-9,"Refineries owned by Valero Energy Corp in Houston, Motiva Inc in Port Arthur, and Exxon Mobile Corp in Baytown, were among the facilities that had reported spills, according to White. Representatives for those companies did not immediately respond to requests for comment."
Exxon,2017-9,Officials also reported spills at Kinder Morgan Inc's Pasadena fuel storage terminal and at an oil terminal in Texas City owned by NuStar Energy LP .
Exxon,2017-9,Kinder Morgan spokeswoman Lexey Long said on Monday the company reported a spill of 500 barrels of gasoline on Aug. 27. Workers covered the spill with a foam blanket and set up a barrier to keep the public away.
Exxon,2017-9,"NuStar spokesman Chris Cho said a small amount of petroleum contact water spilled out of a storage tank into a containment area and was quickly cleaned up. ""There were no injuries and no environmental impact,"" he said."
Exxon,2017-9,Two wastewater treatment plants - Integrity Golden Triangle Marine Services of Port Arthur and San Jacinto River and Rail in Beaumont - also appeared on the list of spill response locations that EPA provided to Reuters.
Exxon,2017-9,"A San Jacinto River and Rail spokesman said the plant had spilled a ""foamy emulsion"" when floodwaters overtopped the berms around its facility but its operators did not expect any health or environmental impacts."
Exxon,2017-9,"Integrity Golden Triangle President Robert Goolsby said a wastewater pit at his plant overflowed into a concrete moat designed to contain such spills, and plant workers were already cleaning it up when state regulators and the Coast Guard arrived."
Exxon,2017-9,"The liquid spills come in addition to more than a million pounds of toxic emissions above legal limits that spewed from industrial facilities following Harvey, according to reports from companies filed with the Texas Commission for Environmental Quality."
Exxon,2017-9,"The EPA and other authorities had warned people affected by the flood that waters could contain bacteria and toxic chemicals, but have said little yet about the specific origins or quantities of substances."
Exxon,2017-9,"Residents in Baytown, where houses sit along the Houston Ship Channel next to several major refineries and chemical plants, said they were concerned about the impact of the spills and releases on health."
Exxon,2017-9,"""I'm against the sword and the wall, what can I do?"" said Carlos Caban, one of the residents, whose son had taken pictures of contaminated-looking floodwaters in nearby refinery site."
Exxon,2017-9,"Several residents reported seeing a metallic sheen on water flowing near the plants during the heaviest flooding, posting videos to YouTube."
Exxon,2017-9,"US Coast Guard, EPA cleaning up a dozen Texas chemical spills after Harvey - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170911T182441.073+0000}}US Coast Guard, EPA cleaning up a dozen Texas chemical spills after HarveyBy Emily Flitter"
Exxon,2017-9,"HOUSTON, Sept 11 (Reuters) - The U.S. Coast Guard and the Environmental Protection Agency are working with Texas state regulators to clean up oil and chemicals spilled from a dozen industrial facilities after flooding from Hurricane Harvey, authorities said."
Exxon,2017-9,"The spills came from oil refineries, fuel terminals and other businesses, but EPA spokeswoman Terri White said it was not possible to provide an estimate for the amounts spilled."

Exxon,2017-9,"""Some is on our property and some is on adjacent property which has already been cleaned up,"" said spokesman Dennis Winkler. ""We do not expect a long-term environmental impact. We do not expect there will be any air impact or health impacts."""
Exxon,2017-9,Representatives from Integrity Golden Triangle did not immediately respond to requests for comment.
Exxon,2017-9,"The liquid spills come in addition to more than a million pounds of toxic emissions above legal limits that spewed from industrial facilities following Harvey, according to reports from companies filed with the Texas Commission for Environmental Quality."

Exxon,2017-9,UPDATE 1-ExxonMobil slashes LNG price to India in bad omen for producers - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,{{20170911T072523.003+0000}}UPDATE 1-ExxonMobil slashes LNG price to India in bad omen for producers* ExxonMobil agrees to renegotiate 20-year LNG contract
Exxon,2017-9,"MELBOURNE/NEW DELHI, Sept 11 (Reuters) - India has won a price cut on a 20-year liquefied natural gas (LNG) deal with global giant ExxonMobil Corp in a rare contract renegotiation, a bad sign for producers in a heavily oversupplied global market."
Exxon,2017-9,"In a trade-off for ExxonMobil, India's Petronet LNG will increase its volumes from the Gorgon LNG project in Australia by an extra 1 million tonnes a year to about 2.5 million tonnes a year, but at cheaper rates than initially agreed in 2009."
Exxon,2017-9,"Long-term contracts are rarely revised in the LNG market, and for a big producer to cave in shows how supply from new plants in Australia and the United States over the past two years has transformed the market, analysts said."
Exxon,2017-9,"""This trend is overall a negative for sellers, as they are forced to provide more flexibility to buyers' needs to maintain their markets,"" said Saul Kavonic, an analyst with energy consultants Wood Mackenzie."
Exxon,2017-9,"India has been aggressive in seeking cheaper deals, also renegotiating a contract with Qatar in 2015, but the real pain for producers would come if major Asian buyers in Japan, Korea and China followed suit."
Exxon,2017-9,"""Happy to share good news that India has, yet again been able to address the long term price issue of LNG from Gorgon to suit Indian market,"" India's oil minister, Dharmendra Pradhan, said on Saturday on social media."
Exxon,2017-9,"Indian consumers would soon receive LNG at an ""amicable price"", Pradhan said. India started receiving Gorgon supplies from January this year."
Exxon,2017-9,"Petronet said in a stock exchange announcement on Monday it had reached a ""broad understanding of terms"" with ExxonMobil, without giving further details."
Exxon,2017-9,"Citing market sources, RBC analyst Ben Wilson estimated ExxonMobil would receive 15 percent less revenue per unit on its sales to Petronet under the new deal."
Exxon,2017-9,"If ExxonMobil had not agreed to renegotiate, Petronet might have scrapped the agreement, leaving the major to pursue damages and resell the volumes on a weak spot market."
Exxon,2017-9,"""They've probably taken the lesser of two evils,"" said Wilson, adding that it did not bode well for other LNG producers such as Australia's Woodside Petroleum which has targeted India to diversify its heavy exposure to Japan and South Korea."
Exxon,2017-9,"In a major shift from previous contractual terms, Exxon has agreed to absorb shipping charges, two sources with knowledge of the matter told Reuters."
Exxon,2017-9,"The original LNG supplies would be priced at less than 14 percent of the Brent oil price, down from about 14.5 percent earlier, while the additional supplies would be priced about 12.5 percent of Brent, the sources said."
Exxon,2017-9,"ExxonMobil, which controls about a quarter of the 15.6 million tonnes a year Gorgon project, had no immediate comment."
Exxon,2017-9,Analysts said the fact India had managed to force ExxonMobil to renegotiate was the latest proof that buyers have the upper hand in a market where LNG spot prices are well below oil-linked contract prices that were signed during the oil boom.
Exxon,2017-9,"""The risk of price renegotiations will become more acute over the next couple years as spot LNG prices remain depressed, even if oil linked prices rise,"" Wood Mackenzie's Kavonic said."
Exxon,2017-9,"""The elephant in the room will be how negotiations play out with traditional markets in Japan and Korea, and especially the Chinese national oil companies."""

Exxon,2017-9,India Petronet set to buy extra 1 mln T Australian LNG from Exxon - sources - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170911T055125.461+0000}}India Petronet set to buy extra 1 mln T Australian LNG from Exxon - sourcesNEW DELHI, Sept 11 (Reuters) - India's Petronet LNG has agreed to buy an additional one million tonnes of liquefied natural gas (LNG) from ExxonMobil's share of the Gorgon project in Australia, two sources said on Monday, after the global giant eased the terms of a previous deal."
Exxon,2017-9,"Petronet will buy the LNG on delivered basis with a price equivalent to about 12.5 percent of Brent oil prices, the sources said. The deal for additional volumes is yet to be signed."
Exxon,2017-9,Indian Oil minister Dharmendra Pradhan said on Saturday that Petronet has been able to renegotiate a contract agreed in 2009 for around 1.5 million tonnes a year of LNG from ExxonMobil's share of the Gorgon LNG project in Australia.[nL4N1LQ0CS]

Exxon,2017-9,ExxonMobil slashes 20-year LNG price to India in bad omen for producers - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170911T025139.966+0000}}ExxonMobil slashes 20-year LNG price to India in bad omen for producers* Petronet gets roughly 15 pct price cut, analyst says"
Exxon,2017-9,"MELBOURNE, Sept 11 (Reuters) - India has won a big price cut on a 20-year liquefied natural gas (LNG) deal with global giant ExxonMobil Corp in a rare contract renegotiation, a bad sign for global producers in a heavily oversupplied market."
Exxon,2017-9,"Long-term contracts are rarely revised in the LNG market, and for a big producer to cave in shows how supply from new plants in Australia and the United States over the past two years has transformed the market, analysts said."
Exxon,2017-9,"""This trend is overall a negative for sellers, as they are forced to provide more flexibility to buyers' needs to maintain their markets,"" said Saul Kavonic, an analyst with energy consultants Wood Mackenzie."
Exxon,2017-9,"India has been aggressive in seeking cheaper deals, also renegotiating a contract with Qatar in 2015, but the real pain for producers would come if major Asian buyers in Japan, Korea and China followed suit."
Exxon,2017-9,"India's oil minister, Dharmendra Pradhan, said on Saturday the country had been able to renegotiate a contract agreed in 2009 for around 1.5 million tonnes a year of LNG from ExxonMobil's share of the Gorgon LNG project in Australia going to Petronet LNG . [nL4N1LQ0BG]"
Exxon,2017-9,"""Happy to share good news that India has, yet again been able to address the long term price issue of LNG from Gorgon to suit Indian market,"" Pradhan said on social media."
Exxon,2017-9,"Indian consumers would soon receive LNG at an ""amicable price"", he said. Gorgon began exporting LNG last year."
Exxon,2017-9,"Citing market sources, RBC analyst Ben Wilson estimated ExxonMobil would receive 15 percent less revenue per unit on its sales to Petronet under the new deal."
Exxon,2017-9,"If ExxonMobil had not agreed to renegotiate the contract, Petronet might have scrapped the agreement, leaving the major to pursue damages and resell the volumes on a weak spot market."
Exxon,2017-9,"""They've probably taken the lesser of two evils,"" said Wilson, adding that it did not bode well for other LNG producers such as Australia's Woodside Petroleum which has targeted India to diversify its heavy exposure to Japan and South Korea."
Exxon,2017-9,Analysts said the fact India had managed to force ExxonMobil to renegotiate was the latest proof that buyers have the upper hand in a market where LNG spot prices are well below oil-linked contract prices that were signed during the oil boom.
Exxon,2017-9,"""The risk of price renegotiations will become more acute over the next couple years as spot LNG prices remain depressed, even if oil linked prices rise,"" Wood Mackenzie's Kavonic said."
Exxon,2017-9,"""The elephant in the room will be how negotiations play out with traditional markets in Japan and Korea, and especially the Chinese national oil companies."""
Exxon,2017-9,RPT-UPDATE 1-Will Saudi Aramco deliver world record profit for next year's IPO? - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,{{20170910T060001.729+0000}}RPT-UPDATE 1-Will Saudi Aramco deliver world record profit for next year's IPO?(Repeats with no changes to text)
Exxon,2017-9,"LONDON, Sept 8 (Reuters) - When oil giant Saudi Aramco discloses its financials for the first time next year, it must either surprise investors with world record profits or reduce its aspirations for a $2 trillion valuation in its initial public offering (IPO). [IPO-ARMO.SE]"
Exxon,2017-9,"Investors have long debated whether Aramco could be valued anywhere close to $2 trillion, the figure suggested by Saudi Crown Prince Mohammed bin Salman, who wants to raise cash through the IPO to finance investments aimed at helping wean the world's biggest oil exporting nation off dependency on crude."
Exxon,2017-9,Based on Aramco's oil reserves of 261 billion barrels and a valuation of $7 to $8 per barrel in line with recent industry acquisitions - such as Total's purchase of Maersk's oil assets - Aramco warrants close to the $2 trillion valuation.
Exxon,2017-9,"But that is not the only metric for an energy firm's worth. By other measures, Aramco's target valuation may be challenging."
Exxon,2017-9,Most other metrics for the world's largest oil producing company are simply not known and will not be disclosed until Aramco publishes financial results before the planned IPO in 2018.
Exxon,2017-9,Yet a simple calculation using globally accepted ratios for Aramco's peers - enterprise value versus core earnings (EV/EBITDA) - shows the Saudi firm has to report EBITDA in the region of $130 billion to achieve a $2 trillion valuation.
Exxon,2017-9,"Such an EBITDA figure would be a global first. No firm in any industry has reported earnings before interest, tax, depreciation and amortisation (EBITDA) above $100 billion."
Exxon,2017-9,"By comparison, Apple , the technology giant and the world's most valuable listed firm that is worth more than $830 billion, reported EBITDA of $82 billion in 2015, according to Thomson Reuters Eikon data."
Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon Mobil , the world's largest listed energy firm with a market capitalisation of $365 billion in 2016, reported EBITDA of $23 billion last year, according to Thomson Reuters Eikon data. In 2012, it reported EBITDA of $65 billion - but that was when oil traded well above $100 a barrel. Benchmark Brent crude is now around $54 ."
Exxon,2017-9,"Last year, Exxon traded at EV/EBITDA of more than 15 times, which is high by energy industry standards. If Aramco matched that same high ratio, its core earnings would need to be around $130 billion to achieve its target valuation."
Exxon,2017-9,Aramco would not be drawn when asked to comment on how it would achieve the $2 trillion figure.
Exxon,2017-9,"""This is highly speculative. We do not comment on speculation or rumour,"" the company told Reuters in a statement."
Exxon,2017-9,A Saudi Arabia-based industry source said Aramco's value could not be calculated until the completion of book-building to assess investor appetite.
Exxon,2017-9,"The source said it was misleading to compare Aramco with Exxon, which has less than half the Saudi firm's oil output and not even a 10th of its reserves. EBITDA should not be the only measure, the source added."
Exxon,2017-9,"Nevertheless, Aramco would do well to secure Exxon's high ratios. Investors tend to like Exxon more than other oil firms, handing it ratios that are sometimes more generous than popular technology firms such as Google and Apple."
Exxon,2017-9,"For example, Exxon's rivals Shell , BP and Total trade at EV/EBITDA of around six times. If Aramco was assessed at that level, it would need to show core earnings at an astonishing $330 billion a year to achieve a valuation of $2 trillion."
Exxon,2017-9,"""One thing you never do ahead of an IPO is to tell the market how much the company will be worth as you immediately become hostage to a number or a timetable,"" said a Western investment banker, who was involved in listing another state energy firm."
Exxon,2017-9,"Yet Aramco could prove hugely profitable, given its oil output of about 10 million barrels per day (bpd) and some of the world's cheapest crude recovery rates, alongside its global refinery network that adds further value."
Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon by comparison has less than half Aramco's output - with oil-equivalent production of 4 million bpd in 2016, while the U.S. firm's reserves are a fraction of Aramco's - with proved oil-equivalent reserves of about 20 billion barrels."
Exxon,2017-9,"Aramco has never published results, but conclusions about its earnings can be drawn from Saudi Arabia's accounts, given oil constitutes the lion's share of the nation's revenues, said Fareed Mohamedi, chief economist at U.S.-based Rapidan Group."
Exxon,2017-9,"""Based on the Saudi current-account balance, Aramco had revenues of $160 billion last year from just oil and refined products exports when the average price of oil was $43 a barrel,"" Mohamedi said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Financials aside, investors will also assess country risk when working out Aramco's valuation."
Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon benefits from having its headquarters in the United States, even if some of its operations and production are in politically unstable nations."
Exxon,2017-9,"Aramco's head office is in Saudi Arabia, a nation in a volatile region with a war in Yemen on its doorstep."
Exxon,2017-9,"""Aramco is definitely a fantastic, modern and high-quality company,"" said the Western banker. ""But unfortunately, no one can say that Saudi Arabia is a fantastic country from the geopolitical prospect."""
Exxon,2017-9,India renegotiates LNG deal with Exxon - oil minister - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170909T193412.520+0000}}India renegotiates LNG deal with Exxon - oil minister* India to get Gorgon LNG at ""amicable price"" soon- minister"
Exxon,2017-9,"NEW DELHI, Sept 9 (Reuters) - India has renegotiated the pricing of liquefied natural gas (LNG) imported from Australia's Gorgon project to make the imported fuel affordable to price-sensitive domestic customers, Indian oil minister Dharmendra Pradhan said on Saturday."
Exxon,2017-9,India has been trying to leverage its position as one of the biggest energy consumers to strike better bargains for its companies. In 2015 it renegotiated the LNG pricing formula with Qatar's Rasgas to buy the gas at half the original price.
Exxon,2017-9,"""Indian customers will receive (Gorgon) LNG volumes at an amicable price soon. This is done in a similar way to what we did with LNG from Qatar,"" Pradhan said in a tweet."
Exxon,2017-9,India's top gas importer Petronet LNG signed a deal in 2009 with Exxon Mobil Corp to buy 1.5 million tonnes of LNG annually from Gorgon for 20 years. At that time Petronet agreed to buy LNG at a cost equivalent to 14.5 percent of the oil price and to pay for the shipping freight as well.
Exxon,2017-9,"Supplies under the deal began from January 2017, with the landed price of gas costing about $11-$13 per million British thermal units (mmBtu), almost double that of Asian spot LNG prices."
Exxon,2017-9,"The Gorgon gas prices are now linked to about 13-13.5 percent of the global oil price on a delivered basis, two sources with knowledge of the negotiation said."
Exxon,2017-9,Renegotiation of the deal also shows how softening oil prices and a global supply glut are forcing LNG exporters to offer better deals to retain their share in global energy markets.
Exxon,2017-9,India wants to gradually move to a gas-based economy and aims to double the cleaner fuel's share in its energy mix to 15 percent in the next few years.
Exxon,2017-9,Petronet's managing director Prabhat Singh declined comment and Pradhan did not specify changes in the pricing formula.
Exxon,2017-9,"""Happy to share good news that India has, yet again, been able to address the long-term price issue of LNG from Gorgon to suit Indian market,"" Pradhan said in a tweet."

Exxon,2017-9,"REFILE-RPT-Harvey may pinch some Gulf Coast refining, chemical projects  - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170908T214817.398+0000}}REFILE-RPT-Harvey may pinch some Gulf Coast refining, chemical projects (Corrects spelling of compete in second paragraph)"
Exxon,2017-9,"NEW YORK/HOUSTON, Sept 8 (Reuters) - Oil and petrochemical plants along the U.S. Gulf Coast intend to go ahead with plans for near record spending on expansions next year, despite Hurricane Harvey driving up labor costs and slowing work, experts said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Harvey largely spared oil and petrochemical plants along the U.S. Gulf Coast from significant damage but thousands of homes and businesses were not as fortunate. Refiners and recovery projects will compete for the same labor, driving up costs or causing labor shortages."
Exxon,2017-9,"Industrial investment in the Gulf Coast is expected to hit $51.9 billion next year, near the 2015 peak, requiring an army of pipefitters, ironworkers and other craftsman, said Industrial Information Resources (IIR), which tracks labor supply for refiners and other industrial companies."
Exxon,2017-9,"""We had a labor shortage before Harvey, but now it's significantly worse,"" said IIR's Anthony Salemme. ""It's going to spread to soft crafts like painters and insulators."""
Exxon,2017-9,Investments have soared in recent years because the shale revolution fed off an existing infrastructure. The region's deep water ports and expanding pipeline and storage networks offer an easy outlet to global markets. It also boasts a welcoming regulatory climate and skilled workforce.
Exxon,2017-9,"Since 2010, $85 billion worth of petrochemical projects have started or been completed across the United States, nearly all of them in the Gulf Coast region, according to the American Chemistry Council."
Exxon,2017-9,"But the concentration along the Gulf of Mexico leaves these facilities and supporting networks exposed to the brutal force of tropical storms and hurricanes, as Harvey laid bare last month."
Exxon,2017-9,"The storm shut roughly a quarter of the nation's refinery capacity and more than a dozen petrochemical plants halted operations. Ports were closed and key fuel pipelines serving the Midwest and U.S. Northeast were partially or completely shut, driving up pump prices as fears of fuel shortages took hold."
Exxon,2017-9,Preliminary assessments suggest that storm's hit to the region is not deterring companies from going ahead with existing projects. But global commodities buyers such as Ineos Group [INEOSG.UL] and Reliance Industries Ltd that relied on existing facilities shut by the storm may now consider putting some warehouses and stock elsewhere.
Exxon,2017-9,"""The robustness of the supply chain is brought a little more under attention,"" said David Witte, a senior vice president at consultants IHS Markit. ""They may be looking at it differently."""
Exxon,2017-9,"There is no sign that major new projects are under threat. Several with plans on the drawing board, including BASF SE , DowDuPont Inc and Exxon Mobil Corp are sticking to growth plans. Others said they will repair Harvey's damage before making any decisions on long-term strategy for the region."
Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon earlier this year said it would invest $20 billion to expand Texas refining and petrochemical operations in Beaumont, Corpus Christi and Baytown. All three communities were damaged by Harvey. [nL8N1LL480]"
Exxon,2017-9,"As part of that expansion, Exxon and Saudi Basic Industries Corp <2010.SE> are proposing an about $10 billion chemical plant in Corpus Christi, near where Harvey made landfall. The project is moving forward, according to a source familiar with the matter."
Exxon,2017-9,"DowDuPont is also undeterred from an ongoing $4 billion expansion project that includes new capacity in Freeport, Texas, on the coast. ""Hurricane Harvey does not change our perspective on the region being a great location for our investments,"" spokeswoman Rachelle Schikorra said in a statement."
Exxon,2017-9,"Royal Dutch Shell Plc , which is expanding its operations in the Gulf, also has proposed new investments in western Pennsylvania, near the natural gas-rich Marcellus formation."
Exxon,2017-9,"The plant will help Shell capture a larger share of the U.S. market for polyethylene, more than half of which is concentrated in northern states. It took Shell years to make the decision to build the plant."
Exxon,2017-9,"Pennsylvania has started to position itself as a second U.S. refining region, even though new plants are years away from opening. The state lacks the specialized refining workforce and proximity to open water - and the Panama Canal - that make the Gulf Coast area still so appealing."
Exxon,2017-9,"The U.S. Gulf Coast will remain an attractive investment area, said Shell spokesman Curtis Smith and other energy officials."
Exxon,2017-9,"""What this storm has demonstrated is the resilience of the energy system,"" said Torgrim Reitan, who runs Statoil ASA's U.S. operations. ""Even a Harvey can't take out this capacity."""

Exxon,2017-9,EXCLUSIVE-BP's stake in giant Azeri oilfields set to fall -sources - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,{{20170908T140550.386+0000}}EXCLUSIVE-BP's stake in giant Azeri oilfields set to fall -sourcesBy Margarita Antidze
Exxon,2017-9,"TBILISI/BAKU, Sept 8 (Reuters) - BP's stake in Azerbaijan's vast oilfields is expected to shrink under a new production-sharing agreement with state energy company SOCAR, two industry sources familiar with the talks told Reuters."
Exxon,2017-9,Azerbaijan plans to sign a new contract with BP next week on development of the giant Azeri-Chirag-Guneshli (ACG) oilfields that will run until 2050.
Exxon,2017-9,The fields are the largest oilfields in the Azerbaijan sector of the Caspian basin.
Exxon,2017-9,An existing deal is due to expire in 2024 and a BP-led consortium and SOCAR signed a letter of intent in December to continue development of the oilfields until 2050 in a move to unlock billions of dollars of fresh investment.
Exxon,2017-9,"""According to preliminary information, SOCAR will increase its share at the expense of a share reduction of other companies, including BP,"" an industry source aware of the negotiations told Reuters."
Exxon,2017-9,"Another industry source, who also is familiar with the talks and did not want to be identified, said SOCAR's share could increase to 20 percent from the current 11.6 percent while BP's share could fall to 30 percent from 35.8 percent."
Exxon,2017-9,"""The shares of some other companies might be also reduced,"" the source said. The figures in the final contract might still change, the source said."
Exxon,2017-9,"A spokeswoman for BP in Azerbaijan said: ""We don't have information on the content of the contract now."""
Exxon,2017-9,"The shareholders in the consortium include BP, SOCAR, Chevron , INPEX <1605.T>, Statoil , ExxonMobil , TPAO, ITOCHU <8001.T> and ONGC Videsh ."
Exxon,2017-9,"The sources said that BP would remain the project operator, although some of its existing rights might be delegated to SOCAR."
Exxon,2017-9,BP came under fire from Azeri President Ilham Aliyev earlier this decade for lower than promised output.
Exxon,2017-9,"Oil output at ACG totalled 14 million tonnes in the first half of 2017, or 585,000 barrels per day, down from 16 million tonnes a year earlier."
Exxon,2017-9,"BUENOS AIRES, Sept 8 (Reuters) - Indigenous Mapuche communities demanding cash payments and blocking oil wells in Argentina's Vaca Muerta area are threatening the long delayed development of the world's second-largest shale fields, oil companies say."
Exxon,2017-9,"Since the beginning of the year the Mapuche have cut off access to 14 wells in the Loma de la Lata field, one of only two shale fields currently producing in the Belgium-sized Vaca Muerta area, state-run YPF said in an e-mailed statement."
Exxon,2017-9,The conflict is intensifying as President Mauricio Macri prioritizes attracting energy investment to develop the area and end Argentina's reliance on imported energy.
Exxon,2017-9,"""It affects us a lot,"" YPF Chairman Miguel Gutierrez said of the Mapuche conflict in a recent interview. ""It's a situation that has been developing for many years and now it must be resolved."""
Exxon,2017-9,A private oil company source who was not authorized to speak on the record said Mapuche communities are eyeing a greater share of the expected boom in the form of cash payments.
Exxon,2017-9,"Companies including Exxon Mobil Corp , France's Total SA , BP PLC unit Pan American Energy LLC and Royal Dutch Shell PLC have announced investments in Vaca Muerta in recent months."
Exxon,2017-9,"Part of Loma de la Lata field is on government-recognized Mapuche territory. Argentine law gives companies the right to extract natural resources found beneath private property, and the state compensates the owner for use of the land."
Exxon,2017-9,"""Imagine you find yourself overnight with 10 drilling towers in the yard of your house and you see them throwing polluted water on either side and breaking everything,"" he said in an interview, adding that members of his community have cancer and seen the number of abortions rise."
Exxon,2017-9,The private company source said the Mapuche also demand companies hire certain private contractors that charge more than the market rate. Cherqui could not be reached to respond to that point.
Exxon,2017-9,"The Argentine government's relationship with the broader Mapuche community has grown tense in recent weeks as human rights groups accuse federal security forces in the disappearance of a man from a Mapuche rights protest in the Patagonian province of Chubut. He has not been seen for over a month, spurring nationwide protests. The government says it is investigating. [nL1N1KX1DA]"
Exxon,2017-9,"YPF's Gutierrez said companies had called on the provincial government of Neuquen, where Loma de la Lata is located, to mediate a solution. Companies had previously negotiated access to wells directly with the Mapuche. The Neuquen government did not respond the request for comment."
Exxon,2017-9,"""What we have to achieve is a protocol to follow and all the parties know: the Mapuches, the industry and regulatory authorities,"" he said."
Exxon,2017-9,"""We are starting a ramping up of development in Vaca Muerta. There is a great opportunity and we have to standardize this type of dialogue."""
Exxon,2017-9,India renegotiates LNG deal with Exxon - oil minister - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170909T193412.520+0000}}India renegotiates LNG deal with Exxon - oil minister* India to get Gorgon LNG at ""amicable price"" soon- minister"
Exxon,2017-9,"NEW DELHI, Sept 9 (Reuters) - India has renegotiated the pricing of liquefied natural gas (LNG) imported from Australia's Gorgon project to make the imported fuel affordable to price-sensitive domestic customers, Indian oil minister Dharmendra Pradhan said on Saturday."
Exxon,2017-9,India has been trying to leverage its position as one of the biggest energy consumers to strike better bargains for its companies. In 2015 it renegotiated the LNG pricing formula with Qatar's Rasgas to buy the gas at half the original price.
Exxon,2017-9,"""Indian customers will receive (Gorgon) LNG volumes at an amicable price soon. This is done in a similar way to what we did with LNG from Qatar,"" Pradhan said in a tweet."
Exxon,2017-9,India's top gas importer Petronet LNG signed a deal in 2009 with Exxon Mobil Corp to buy 1.5 million tonnes of LNG annually from Gorgon for 20 years. At that time Petronet agreed to buy LNG at a cost equivalent to 14.5 percent of the oil price and to pay for the shipping freight as well.
Exxon,2017-9,"Supplies under the deal began from January 2017, with the landed price of gas costing about $11-$13 per million British thermal units (mmBtu), almost double that of Asian spot LNG prices."
Exxon,2017-9,"The Gorgon gas prices are now linked to about 13-13.5 percent of the global oil price on a delivered basis, two sources with knowledge of the negotiation said."
Exxon,2017-9,Renegotiation of the deal also shows how softening oil prices and a global supply glut are forcing LNG exporters to offer better deals to retain their share in global energy markets.
Exxon,2017-9,India wants to gradually move to a gas-based economy and aims to double the cleaner fuel's share in its energy mix to 15 percent in the next few years.
Exxon,2017-9,Petronet's managing director Prabhat Singh declined comment and Pradhan did not specify changes in the pricing formula.
Exxon,2017-9,"""Happy to share good news that India has, yet again, been able to address the long-term price issue of LNG from Gorgon to suit Indian market,"" Pradhan said in a tweet."

But global commodities buyers such as Ineos Group [INEOSG.UL] and Reliance Industries Ltd that relied on existing facilities shut by the storm may now consider putting some warehouses and stock elsewhere.
Exxon,2017-9,"""The robustness of the supply chain is brought a little more under attention,"" said David Witte, a senior vice president at consultants IHS Markit. ""They may be looking at it differently."""
Exxon,2017-9,"There is no sign that major new projects are under threat. Several with plans on the drawing board, including BASF SE , DowDuPont Inc and Exxon Mobil Corp are sticking to growth plans. Others said they will repair Harvey's damage before making any decisions on long-term strategy for the region."
Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon earlier this year said it would invest $20 billion to expand Texas refining and petrochemical operations in Beaumont, Corpus Christi and Baytown. All three communities were damaged by Harvey. [nL8N1LL480]"
Exxon,2017-9,"As part of that expansion, Exxon and Saudi Basic Industries Corp <2010.SE> are proposing an about $10 billion chemical plant in Corpus Christi, near where Harvey made landfall. The project is moving forward, according to a source familiar with the matter."
Exxon,2017-9,"DowDuPont is also undeterred from an ongoing $4 billion expansion project that includes new capacity in Freeport, Texas, on the coast. ""Hurricane Harvey does not change our perspective on the region being a great location for our investments,"" spokeswoman Rachelle Schikorra said in a statement."
Exxon,2017-9,"Royal Dutch Shell Plc , which is expanding its operations in the Gulf, also has proposed new investments in western Pennsylvania, near the natural gas-rich Marcellus formation."
Exxon,2017-9,"The plant will help Shell capture a larger share of the U.S. market for polyethylene, more than half of which is concentrated in northern states. It took Shell years to make the decision to build the plant."
Exxon,2017-9,"Pennsylvania has started to position itself as a second U.S. refining region, even though new plants are years away from opening. The state lacks the specialized refining workforce and proximity to open water - and the Panama Canal - that make the Gulf Coast area still so appealing."
Exxon,2017-9,"The U.S. Gulf Coast will remain an attractive investment area, said Shell spokesman Curtis Smith and other energy officials."
Exxon,2017-9,"""What this storm has demonstrated is the resilience of the energy system,"" said Torgrim Reitan, who runs Statoil ASA's U.S. operations. ""Even a Harvey can't take out this capacity."""

Exxon,2017-9,"TBILISI/BAKU, Sept 8 (Reuters) - BP's stake in Azerbaijan's vast oilfields is expected to shrink under a new production-sharing agreement with state energy company SOCAR, two industry sources familiar with the talks told Reuters."

Exxon,2017-9,The fields are the largest oilfields in the Azerbaijan sector of the Caspian basin.
Exxon,2017-9,An existing deal is due to expire in 2024 and a BP-led consortium and SOCAR signed a letter of intent in December to continue development of the oilfields until 2050 in a move to unlock billions of dollars of fresh investment.
Exxon,2017-9,"""According to preliminary information, SOCAR will increase its share at the expense of a share reduction of other companies, including BP,"" an industry source aware of the negotiations told Reuters."
Exxon,2017-9,"Another industry source, who also is familiar with the talks and did not want to be identified, said SOCAR's share could increase to 20 percent from the current 11.6 percent while BP's share could fall to 30 percent from 35.8 percent."
Exxon,2017-9,"""The shares of some other companies might be also reduced,"" the source said. The figures in the final contract might still change, the source said."

Exxon,2017-9,"Oil output at ACG totalled 14 million tonnes in the first half of 2017, or 585,000 barrels per day, down from 16 million tonnes a year earlier."

Exxon,2017-9,"""Imagine you find yourself overnight with 10 drilling towers in the yard of your house and you see them throwing polluted water on either side and breaking everything,"" he said in an interview, adding that members of his community have cancer and seen the number of abortions rise."

Exxon,2017-9,INSIGHT-The next oil major? Service firm Schlumberger's big bet on production - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,{{20170908T050004.131+0000}}INSIGHT-The next oil major? Service firm Schlumberger's big bet on productionBy Liz Hampton
Exxon,2017-9,"HOUSTON, Sept 8 (Reuters) - The world's largest oilfield services company, Schlumberger NV , is spending billions of dollars buying stakes in its customers' oil and gas projects - investing in the same ventures it supplies with equipment and expertise."
Exxon,2017-9,"The new business model gives Schlumberger a say in drilling decisions, oilfield management and even on hiring other Schlumberger units for service contracts, the company has told investors."
Exxon,2017-9,The expanded operational authority saves Schlumberger from bidding for each of the many jobs that typically require separate contracts on a large drilling project - effectively locking out the firm's competitors.
Exxon,2017-9,"Schlumberger's gamble could upend the service business model throughout the industry, as rivals including General Electric Co's unit Baker Hughes say they are considering whether to adopt similar strategies."
Exxon,2017-9,"The model can supercharge profits on a given job but also ramps up risk, giving the firm more exposure to global oil price swings and potentially big losses if individual projects fail. The downsides have some analysts questioning whether the traditionally conservative firm is taking on too many speculative projects too quickly."
Exxon,2017-9,"Schlumberger already has taken hundreds of millions in write-downs or impairments on some of these joint ventures, according to its financial filings."
Exxon,2017-9,"Traditionally, oil producers manage the risk and make the financial and operational decisions on projects; they pay service providers a fee to carry out individual jobs. Firms such as Schlumberger typically supply a wide variety of services, such as well design, along with technology and staff to run rigs."
Exxon,2017-9,Schlumberger declined to make executives available for interviews and did not respond to written questions about its production business.
Exxon,2017-9,"Despite early setbacks, Schlumberger has committed cash to growing the division, called Schlumberger Production Management, since its launch in 2011. Last year, it generated $1.4 billion in revenue. It had investment of $2.6 billion as of June 30, Schlumberger Executive Vice President Patrick Schorn told investors earlier this summer."
Exxon,2017-9,"The company's investments have the firm co-managing about 230,000 barrels a day of oil and gas output at the end of 2016 - about as much as one of the largest U.S. independent producers, Pioneer Natural Resources ."
Exxon,2017-9,"This year, the company stepped up the financing role, opening a standalone investment fund to provide financing for the ventures. The company has not disclosed the size of the fund."
Exxon,2017-9,Such ventures require a breadth of skills and a tolerance for risk generally found at large integrated oil companies such as Chevron Corp and Exxon Mobil Corp .
Exxon,2017-9,Two of Schlumberger's newest partnerships - a deepwater liquefied natural gas project off the coast of Equatorial Guinea and an Argentina shale development with YPF SA - involve decision-making and operational authority similar to that typically held by multinational oil producers.
Exxon,2017-9,"In June, Schlumberger agreed to invest $700 million in an oil exploration project with Nigerian National Petroleum Corp and First Exploration & Production that would require global oil prices of between $50 to $60 a barrel to achieve a 20 percent profit, research house Bernstein estimated in a report published in July. Current prices are struggling to break out of the bottom of that range."
Exxon,2017-9,"As Schlumberger's production business has grown, it has negotiated deals that include equity in oil and gas fields and as well as deals that give the firm payment based on oil and gas output, according to interviews with customers, partners, investors and former Schlumberger executives."
Exxon,2017-9,"Schlumberger this year agreed to contribute $390 million for a 49 percent stake in a venture with YPF in Argentina's Vaca Muerta shale field, which has attracted international oil firms including Chevron and Royal Dutch Shell ."
Exxon,2017-9,Schlumberger Chief Executive Paal Kibsgaard has downplayed the potential for its production business to compete with its own oil company customers.
Exxon,2017-9,"He described the enterprise as ""a new avenue for project investments alongside our customers"" in remarks to investors in April."
Exxon,2017-9,"Schorn also insisted this spring that the business is ""not significantly changing the risk profile ... the biggest risk remains the cyclical nature"" of the oil and gas industry."
Exxon,2017-9,"Investors say Schlumberger, which held $6.22 billion in cash and short-term investments at June 30, is strong enough to handle any increased risks and the price volatility of its investments in long-term projects."
Exxon,2017-9,"As both project manager and service provider, Schlumberger also has an enviable level of control over operations, said Mike Breard of Dallas-based wealth management firm Hodges Capital, which invests in oilfield service companies."
Exxon,2017-9,"British-based natural gas explorer Sound Energy PLC was happy to give Schlumberger full rights to the service contracts on drilling projects in Morocco in exchange for a Schlumberger investment amounting to 27 percent of total costs, said the chief of British-based natural gas explorer."
Exxon,2017-9,Schlumberger will get 27.5 percent of revenue from the oil produced.
Exxon,2017-9,"""We're smaller and entrepreneurial. Schlumberger has the technical capability and cash. That's the nature of the partnership,"" Sound CEO James Parsons said in an interview."
Exxon,2017-9,The duo has completed three wells in Morocco and plans to drill three more by year end.
Exxon,2017-9,"""It's a $50 [million] or $60 million bet for them so far,"" Parsons said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Schlumberger's appetite for these ventures is spurring rivals to consider similar financing and services deals. Baker Hughes recently agreed to provide about $10 million in financing to Twinza Oil's first offshore gas field in Papua New Guinea, supplying the cash to prove the merits of the field."
Exxon,2017-9,"""It allows Twinza to have success in going out to raise financing,"" Baker Hughes CEO Lorenzo Simonelli said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Baker Hughes will not take a stake in the oilfield, unlike some of Schlumberger's joint investments with producers."
Exxon,2017-9,"In 2014 and 2015, Schlumberger took nearly $400 million in combined write-offs on oil production investments, including an Eagle Ford shale field in south Texas that struggled after oil prices crashed."
Exxon,2017-9,"It also is owed about $900 million by Ecuador. In July, the South American country said it had negotiated a payment plan that includes an expanded contract that has Schlumberger agreeing to invest another $1 billion in the venture."
Exxon,2017-9,Schlumberger hasn't commented on the South American nation's disclosure. It previously acknowledged taking Ecuadorian bonds in lieu of cash for $150 million in bills. It also previously estimated its investment in the projects at up to $4.9 billion over 20 years.
Exxon,2017-9,The write downs have stirred some on Wall Street to question whether Schlumberger should take more conservative path with its oil production partnerships.
Exxon,2017-9,"The firm's production division ""used to focus on production management of well understood low-risk oil fields,"" said Colin Davies, a Bernstein oilfield services analyst. ""Now it has expanded into frankly somewhat more speculative ventures."""

Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon, other refiners buy fuel as plants recover slowly from Harvey - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170907T230624.729+0000}}Exxon, other refiners buy fuel as plants recover slowly from HarveyBy Devika Krishna Kumar and Jessica Resnick-Ault"
Exxon,2017-9,"Sept 7 (Reuters) - Refiners including Exxon Mobil Corp and Motiva Enterprises purchased fuel on Thursday to compensate for lost output from plants that have been shut since Hurricane Harvey hit the U.S. Gulf Coast last month, traders said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Refiners typically sell fuel, rather than buy it. The purchases sparked concern in the market that Harvey may have inflicted damage on refineries that will take time to repair. That pushed up prices on Gulf Coast physical markets by about 5 cents a gallon, five traders familiar with the deals said."
Exxon,2017-9,"The surge in buying also came as refiners scrambled to meet the deadline to ship on Colonial Pipeline, the largest line in the country, during the five-day period through Thursday."
Exxon,2017-9,"Harvey dumped a record amount of rain on refineries in Texas, the heart of the U.S. energy industry. The shutdowns have cut millions of barrels of fuel supplies from the world's largest oil consumer, pushing up prices for gasoline, diesel and jet fuel across the country."
Exxon,2017-9,"Refiners in the Gulf are still assessing the impact of flooding on their plants and would have avoided buying fuel if they could have supplied their customers themselves, traders said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Until Thursday, refiners in the Gulf had only fleetingly bought cargoes in the physical markets since Harvey, traders said."
Exxon,2017-9,"The refiners will ship the fuel through Colonial Pipeline, the main transit route for fuel produced in the Gulf destined for gas stations in cities along the U.S. East Coast such as New York."
Exxon,2017-9,Colonial restarted sections of its main gasoline and distillate lines in Texas earlier this week after a partial shutdown when supplies from Gulf refiners dwindled and floods prevented refiners from loading fuel into the line. [nENN0UWJ8L]
Exxon,2017-9,"It is unclear how much fuel is moving through the line currently, because Colonial does not disclose volumes shipped. [nENN0UWJ8L]"
Exxon,2017-9,"Without the purchases, refiners may have struggled to meet commitments to their branded stores along the East Coast, traders said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Even as refiners struggle to plug supply gaps related to Harvey, new shortages have emerged in the U.S. Southeast as Hurricane Irma disrupted deliveries there. [nL2N1LO119]"
Exxon,2017-9,The two largest refineries in the country were both shut down by Harvey and are projected to partially restart by next week.
Exxon,2017-9,"Motiva aims to have the nation's largest refinery running at 40 percent of capacity by Monday, the company said on Thursday. The plant, at Port Arthur in Texas, has capacity of 603,000 barrels per day (bpd)."
Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon's 560,500 bpd Baytown, Texas, refinery, the second largest, may restart partial production by early next week, sources said. [nL2N1LO0NU] [nL2N1LN2O6]"
Exxon,2017-9,"A second large Exxon plant is also shut at Beaumont in Texas. The two plants combined can process about 920,000 bpd."
Exxon,2017-9,Exxon said on Thursday it was completing minor repairs at Baytown and sources said the company is restarting utilities at Beaumont. [nFWN1LO0QB] [nL2N1LN2KD]
Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon is working to ensure customers are well supplied with gasoline, a spokeswoman said. She did not comment on specific fuel purchases. Motiva declined to comment on trading activity."
Exxon,2017-9,"Harvey shut about 4.4 million barrels per day (bpd) of refining capacity, nearly 24 percent of the U.S. total."
Exxon,2017-9,"As of Thursday, at least 1 million barrels were still shut, with another 3 million barrels of capacity in the process of restarting or running at reduced rates. [nL8N1LL480]"
Exxon,2017-9,"The storm also shut down oil ports and the Houston Ship Channel, one of the main routes for waterborne supplies from refineries. [nFWN1LG0RL]"
Exxon,2017-9,The rise in cash gasoline prices reversed falls earlier this week as some plants began restarting.
Exxon,2017-9,"Conventional gasoline rose 4.50 cents a gallon to trade at a 18 cent-per-gallon premium to benchmark U.S. gasoline futures on the New York Mercantile Exchange , traders said. Benchmark futures ended the session 0.7 percent lower at $1.6610 a gallon."
Exxon,2017-9,The most actively traded Gulf coast gasoline grade is A2 CBOB. Prices for that grade jumped 5 cents to trade 18 cents above the benchmark.

Exxon,2017-9,UPDATE 1-Kazakhstan may strike separate deal with OPEC on oil output curbs - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,{{20170907T132425.316+0000}}UPDATE 1-Kazakhstan may strike separate deal with OPEC on oil output curbs(Writes through with comments on OPEC discussions)
Exxon,2017-9,"ASTANA, Sept 7 (Reuters) - Kazakhstan is aiming for a standalone deal with leading global oil producers on restraining its crude production due to a need to crank up output at its Kashagan field, a Kazakh official said on Thursday."
Exxon,2017-9,"The Central Asian nation increased oil and gas condensate output by 9.9 percent in January-July to 49.907 million tonnes, or 1.724 million barrels per day (bpd), exceeding its quota of 1.7 million bpd under a global supply pact."
Exxon,2017-9,Kazakhstan has said it needs to adjust the terms of the deal as it expects to boost output later this year thanks to the giant Kashagan field. [nR4N1IZ050]
Exxon,2017-9,"On Thursday, Deputy Energy Minister Aset Magauov said his country needed to repay the shareholders in Kashagan, where output had been delayed for years before it was relaunched last year."
Exxon,2017-9,"""I think that talks on Kazakhstan's commitments will continue separately,"" Magauov told reporters."
Exxon,2017-9,"""There is understanding from OPEC that the project (Kashagan) is very large, there have been huge investments and there is a need to return these investments to shareholders."""
Exxon,2017-9,"He said Kashagan, with investments of around $55 billion, was expected to produce 13 million tonnes next year (260,000 bpd), while other oil projects in the country could see their output reduced."
Exxon,2017-9,"Kashagan has been developed by a consortium of China National Petroleum Corp [CNPET.UL], Exxon Mobil , Eni , Royal Dutch Shell , Total , Inpex <1605.T> and KazMunaiGas ."
Exxon,2017-9,"The Organization of the Petroleum Exporting Countries and other producers, including Russia and Kazakhstan, agreed to cut output from January this year until the end of March 2018 to reduce global inventories and support oil prices."
Exxon,2017-9,UPDATE 1-Exxon CEO says making progress restarting refinery in Texas -CNBC - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,{{20170907T122358.642+0000}}UPDATE 1-Exxon CEO says making progress restarting refinery in Texas -CNBC(Adds details on Exxon's post-Harvey plans)
Exxon,2017-9,"Sept 7 (Reuters) - Exxon Mobil Corp is making good progress as it restarts operations at its Baytown, Texas refinery following Hurricane Harvey, Chief Executive Darren Woods told CNBC."
Exxon,2017-9,"The world's largest publicly traded oil producer on Sunday restarted operations at the 560,500-barrel-per-day refinery - the nation's second-largest."
Exxon,2017-9,"""It's very difficult to predict exactly when all those units will be back up and we'll be back on our full load. But we're making good progress. We're hoping to get some units started up later this week, and then it will be one unit after another,"" Woods said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon has not yet assessed Harvey's impact on third quarter earnings, Woods told the TV channel."
Exxon,2017-9,"Harvey tore through Corpus Christi in southern Texas on Aug. 25 and then drenched the Houston area with historic rains, knocking out nearly a fifth of U.S. oil-refining capacity. Oil companies are now bracing for Hurricane Irma, one of the most powerful Atlantic storms in a century. [nL2N1LF0UJ]"
Exxon,2017-9,"Irma has not impacted any of the oil major's offshore Gulf of Mexico operations yet, Woods said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Part of Exxon's Harvey response team has been tasked with planning for Irma, which could make landfall in Florida this weekend, CNBC reported."

Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170907T112834.033+0000}}Exxon CEO says Harvey had bigger impact on Mexico operations - CNBCSept 7 (Reuters) - Exxon Mobil Corp Chief Executive Darren Woods told CNBC on Thursday that Hurricane Harvey had a bigger impact on the company's Mexico operations, and said that Irma had not impacted any of the oil major's offshore operations yet."

Exxon,2017-9,"RPT-Meth, coke and oil: A drug boom in the Texas shale patch - Reuters News"
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170907T110001.600+0000}}RPT-Meth, coke and oil: A drug boom in the Texas shale patch(Repeats for additional clients with no changes to text)"
Exxon,2017-9,"MIDLAND, Texas, Sept 7 (Reuters) - When Joe Forsythe returned to the West Texas oilfields last year after a stint in a drug rehab facility, he figured he had beaten his addiction to methamphetamine."
Exxon,2017-9,The 32-year-old rig worker and equipment handler lasted about a year before relapsing.
Exxon,2017-9,"""It's easy to get back into that mentality,"" said Forsythe, of Midland, Texas, who said he no longer uses drugs after several stints in rehab since 2015. ""I'd work 24 hours ... I was just plagued with fatigue and needed something to improve my work ethic."""
Exxon,2017-9,"Forsythe's experience and others like it reflect a painful flipside of the nation's shale oil boom - a parallel increase in substance abuse, drug crime and related social ills."
Exxon,2017-9,"While drug use is a problem among industrial workers nationwide, it raises particular concern in the oil patch as U.S. production surges to record levels in what is already one of the nation's most dangerous sectors - with a fatality rate about three times the average for other industries, according to 2015 federal statistics."
Exxon,2017-9,"Drug use is a significant factor in workplace injuries and crimes involving oilfield workers, according to drug counselors, hospital and police officials and court records in West Texas, the epicenter of the U.S. shale sector."
Exxon,2017-9,"As the shale revolution has spawned waves of hiring here since 2010, law enforcement authorities have tracked a boom in drug trafficking and related crime. In Midland and Ector counties, home to many Permian Basin oil workers, state and local police in 2016 seized more than 95 pounds of methamphetamine - up from less than four pounds in 2010."
Exxon,2017-9,"Meth and cocaine are stimulants of choice in the oil patch to get though long oilfield shifts, but alcohol and pain killers such as opioids are also widely abused - often to soften the crash after taking stimulants, drug addicts and counselors said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Drug charges in the industry town of Midland more than doubled between 2012 and 2016, to 942 from 491, according to police data. In neighboring Odessa, total drug arrests doubled between 2010 and 2016, to 1291 from 756, according to Odessa Police Department data."
Exxon,2017-9,"The increase in drug crime stretched through two boom periods in the West Texas oil patch, before and after a crude price crash that hit in 2014."
Exxon,2017-9,"Oil companies typically drug test job applicants and often conduct additional random tests on employees. For truck drivers and those involved with hazardous materials, tests are also conducted under federal programs run by the U.S. Department of Transportation."
Exxon,2017-9,Several oil firms with major operations in the Permian Basin declined to discuss how they handle drugs in the oil patch or did not respond to inquiries.
Exxon,2017-9,"Schlumberger NV , Halliburton Co and Exxon Mobil Corp declined to comment. Exxon referred Reuters to its alcohol and drug policy."
Exxon,2017-9,Pioneer Natural Resources Co. and ConocoPhillips did not respond to requests for comment.
Exxon,2017-9,"The American Petroleum Institute, an industry trade group, declined to comment."
Exxon,2017-9,"Despite corporate and regulatory efforts to curb drug abuse, many oilfield workers regularly use stimulants on long shifts of grueling work for relatively high pay, said drug counselors, local law enforcement officials and oil field workers recovering from addictions."
Exxon,2017-9,"More than a third of clients at Midland's Springboard drug rehabilitation center are currently involved in the oil and gas industry, said Executive Director Steve Thomason."
Exxon,2017-9,"Rising oil prices have brought more admissions for methamphetamine abuse, Thomason said."
Exxon,2017-9,"""People say they can work on it for 24 hours straight,"" he said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Long shifts are common in the oil industry because expensive drilling equipment, often leased at high daily rates, runs through the night, and workers often have to commute to wells in remote locations. Most oil producers subcontract oilfield services to smaller companies that are not unionized."
Exxon,2017-9,"Springboard's admissions of methamphetamine users went up 20 percent in the first six months of this year compared with the last half of 2016, he said. The number of rigs operating in the Permian Basin increased more than 38 percent during the same period, according to data from energy services firm Baker Hughes ."
Exxon,2017-9,"Corporal Steve LeSueur, a spokesman for the Odessa police, said the influx of drugs in the oil patch is stretching police resources."
Exxon,2017-9,"In 2016, Shawn Pinson, an employee of a well construction company, was convicted of murdering an acquaintance following a drug-related dispute."
Exxon,2017-9,"The murder occurred around the same time he was arrested for possession of methamphetamine, police records show. The victim tested positive for meth at the time of the murder, according to an autopsy."
Exxon,2017-9,"At his trial, witnesses close to Pinson testified he had become addicted to methamphetamine while working in the oilfield, according to a prosecutor and a defense attorney involved in the case."
Exxon,2017-9,"Pinson did not respond to a letter seeking comment and his current attorney, Michele Greene, did not respond to a request for comment."
Exxon,2017-9,"When oil jobs are plentiful, companies desperate for labor sometimes will disregard signs of substance abuse, said three recovering drug addicts who worked in the oilfield."
Exxon,2017-9,"""These oilfield bosses - they party, too,"" Forsythe said. ""As long as you're getting the job done and not making a scene, they won't drug test you."""
Exxon,2017-9,"One recovering addict, who declined to use his name because he still works in the industry, said he was often high during long-haul trips driving trucks transporting oil."
Exxon,2017-9,"""I could do a little coke and speed and it would give me the extra stretch,"" he said. ""It ended up running me to the ground."""

Exxon,2017-9,Putin rues awarding U.S. top diplomat Tillerson Russian state honour - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170907T084936.092+0000}}Putin rues awarding U.S. top diplomat Tillerson Russian state honourVLADIVOSTOK, Russia, Sept 7 (Reuters) - Vladimir Putin took a jab at Rex Tillerson on Thursday, joking that the U.S. Secretary of State had ""fallen in with the wrong company"" since he had awarded him a Russian state honour for his contribution to Russian-U.S. relations."
Exxon,2017-9,"Hopes of detente in Moscow's relations with Washington under Donald Trump, who had praised President Putin before winning the White House, have faded as the countries have imposed sanctions and expelled diplomats in recent months."
Exxon,2017-9,"Addressing a U.S. citizen at a plenary session of an economic forum in the far eastern city of Vladivostok, Putin said: ""We awarded your compatriot Mr. Tillerson the Order of Friendship, but he seems to have fallen in with the wrong company and to be steering in the other direction."""
Exxon,2017-9,"""I hope that the wind of cooperation, friendship and reciprocity will eventually put him on the right path,"" Putin added, drawing cheers from the crowd."
Exxon,2017-9,"In 2013 Putin awarded Tillerson, then CEO of energy giant Exxon Mobil , the Order of Friendship, a Russian state honour, for his ""significant contribution to strengthening cooperation in the energy sector""."
Exxon,2017-9,"Russia's relations with the United States deteriorated over its annexation of the Black Sea peninsula of Crimea in 2014 and support for pro-Russian separatists in eastern Ukraine, prompting Washington to impose economic sanctions against Moscow."
Exxon,2017-9,"The Kremlin, which has denied U.S. allegations it meddled in the presidential vote, had heaped praise on Trump during his election campaign, saying it supported efforts to improve Russian-American relations."
Exxon,2017-9,"But Trump, who was faced scrutiny over the alleged ties of his entourage with Russia, reluctantly signed into law fresh sanctions against Moscow, further straining relations."

Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170907T070118.976+0000}}Russia's Putin says row with Exxon over Sakhalin-1 is resolvedVLADIVOSTOK, Russia, Sept 7 (Reuters) - A dispute with U.S. major ExxonMobil over the Sakhalin-1 oil and gas project has been resolved, Russian President Vladimir Putin said on Thursday."
Exxon,2017-9,"Speaking at a conference in the Russian Pacific port city of Vladivostok, he said that the government will soon announce the decision."
Exxon,2017-9,Exxon has been in talks with Russian gas giant Gazprom for years over gas sales from Sakhalin-1. Gazprom has a monopoly on gas exports via pipeline from Russia.
Exxon,2017-9,Exxon also lodged a claim with a court of arbitration in Stockholm in 2015 seeking the return of $637 million which it said it had over-paid in taxes to the Russian exchequer.

Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170906T221650.159+0000}}UPDATE 1-Exxon Beaumont refinery beginning to restart utilities -sources(Adds details on units restarting, units shut)"
Exxon,2017-9,"HOUSTON, Sept 6 (Reuters) - ExxonMobil Corp began restarting utilities at the 362,300 barrel per day (bpd) Beaumont, Texas, refinery on Wednesday for the first time in seven days since being shut by Hurricane Harvey, said sources familiar with plant operations."
Exxon,2017-9,Exxon spokeswoman Charlotte Huffaker said the Beaumont refinery remains shut due to flooding within the plant.
Exxon,2017-9,"""Flood waters have receded substantially, and we are continuing impact assessments,"" Huffaker said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon is restarting units like boilers and other utilities needed in the refining process ahead of restarting production units that make motor fuels, the sources said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon said on Sunday it began restarting the polyethylene plant in the Beaumont chemical plant, which adjoins the refinery."
