Africa Crude-Offer levels steady, Sonangol sold out for OctLONDON, Sept 6 (Reuters) - Angolan state oil firm Sonangol was reported by traders on Wednesday to have sold a cargo of Gimboa, the last of its October-loading cargoes for sale, while Nigerian supply remained ample."
Exxon,2017-9,Offer levels for Nigerian and Angolan cargoes were steady and the focus remained on pending Indian buy tenders.
Exxon,2017-9,"* State oil company Sonangol sold a cargo of Gimboa on Monday, its last October cargo, traders said, one of which added that a U.S. buyer had bought the cargo. Price details did not emerge."
Exxon,2017-9,"* About 12 or less Angolan crude cargoes were still available, traders said."
Exxon,2017-9,* Offer levels were steady. Chevron was offering Cabinda at dated Brent plus $1.10 a barrel and Total was offering Girassol at dated Brent plus $1.40.
Exxon,2017-9,"* Just over 30 October-loading cargoes were available for sale, or slightly more than half the loading programme. The number was pegged at 30 on Tuesday."
Exxon,2017-9,"* Offers were steady. ExxonMobil was offering a late-month cargo at dated Brent plus $1.75, a trader said - 10 cents higher than an offer heard last week."
Exxon,2017-9,* The result of Indian refiner BPCL's tender to buy cargoes loading Oct. 25 to Nov. 5 had yet to emerge.
Exxon,2017-9,"* Indian Oil Corp. is running two tenders, the results of which are expected on Thursday. The refiner is seeking a wide variety of grades, with West African sought for loading Nov. 1-10, Nov. 5-20 and Nov. 20-30."

Exxon,2017-9,UPDATE 2-Norway receives more bidders for mature areas oil licensing round - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,{{20170906T103019.170+0000}}UPDATE 2-Norway receives more bidders for mature areas oil licensing round* Norway hands out acreage near existing fields each year
Exxon,2017-9,"OSLO, Sept 6 (Reuters) - Norway's licensing round to explore for oil and gas in mature offshore areas attracted bids from 39 companies, up from 33 firms last year, the Oil and Energy Ministry said on Wednesday."
Exxon,2017-9,"The announcement comes five days before a parliamentary election in Norway, where some opposition parties have called for scaling back exploration to reduce carbon emissions from Western Europe's top oil and gas producer."
Exxon,2017-9,"When the so-called predefined areas (APA) licensing round was announced in May, the right-wing government expanded the areas offered near existing discoveries by 87 blocks in the Norwegian and the Barents Seas."
Exxon,2017-9,Norway's Oil and Energy Minister Terje Soeviknes said in a statement that increased interest in this year's APA round showed optimism was returning to the industry.
Exxon,2017-9,"""Further exploration activity is vital to future value creation and employment,"" he said. ""This in turn is important with reference to financing the welfare state."""
Exxon,2017-9,"Applicants included majors Shell , ConocoPhillips , Exxon Mobil and Total , as well as Norway's biggest oil and gas company Statoil ."
Exxon,2017-9,"Also on the list was Oslo-listed DNO , the biggest oil producer in the Kurdistan region of Iraq, which re-entered the Norwegian continental shelf in May after acquiring Origo Exploration."
Exxon,2017-9,"In the APA round in 2016, 29 of the 33 applicants were awarded 56 production licenses."
Exxon,2017-9,"Mature area licensing rounds attracted the most interest in 2013, when 50 firms submitted bids, compared to 16 bids in 2005."
Exxon,2017-9,"Norway's APA rounds were introduced in 2003 to encourage exploration near existing discoveries. Oil firms usually have between one and three years to decide whether to drill an exploration well, otherwise the production licence becomes void."
Exxon,2017-9,Norway holds separate licensing rounds to hand out acreage in frontier areas.
Exxon,2017-9,"Companies do not pay for exploration acreage, but future profits from any discoveries are subject to high tax rates."

Exxon,2017-9,UPDATE 2-Norway receives more bidders for mature areas oil licensing round - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,{{20170906T103019.170+0000}}UPDATE 2-Norway receives more bidders for mature areas oil licensing round* Norway hands out acreage near existing fields each year
Exxon,2017-9,"OSLO, Sept 6 (Reuters) - Norway's licensing round to explore for oil and gas in mature offshore areas attracted bids from 39 companies, up from 33 firms last year, the Oil and Energy Ministry said on Wednesday."
Exxon,2017-9,"The announcement comes five days before a parliamentary election in Norway, where some opposition parties have called for scaling back exploration to reduce carbon emissions from Western Europe's top oil and gas producer."
Exxon,2017-9,"When the so-called predefined areas (APA) licensing round was announced in May, the right-wing government expanded the areas offered near existing discoveries by 87 blocks in the Norwegian and the Barents Seas."
Exxon,2017-9,Norway's Oil and Energy Minister Terje Soeviknes said in a statement that increased interest in this year's APA round showed optimism was returning to the industry.
Exxon,2017-9,"""Further exploration activity is vital to future value creation and employment,"" he said. ""This in turn is important with reference to financing the welfare state."""
Exxon,2017-9,"Applicants included majors Shell , ConocoPhillips , Exxon Mobil and Total , as well as Norway's biggest oil and gas company Statoil ."
Exxon,2017-9,"Also on the list was Oslo-listed DNO , the biggest oil producer in the Kurdistan region of Iraq, which re-entered the Norwegian continental shelf in May after acquiring Origo Exploration."
Exxon,2017-9,"In the APA round in 2016, 29 of the 33 applicants were awarded 56 production licenses."
Exxon,2017-9,"Mature area licensing rounds attracted the most interest in 2013, when 50 firms submitted bids, compared to 16 bids in 2005."
Exxon,2017-9,"Norway's APA rounds were introduced in 2003 to encourage exploration near existing discoveries. Oil firms usually have between one and three years to decide whether to drill an exploration well, otherwise the production licence becomes void."
Exxon,2017-9,Norway holds separate licensing rounds to hand out acreage in frontier areas.
Exxon,2017-9,"Companies do not pay for exploration acreage, but future profits from any discoveries are subject to high tax rates."
Exxon,2017-9,UPDATE 3-U.S. gasoline prices slip as oil industry bounces back from Harvey - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170904T210245.168+0000}}UPDATE 3-U.S. gasoline prices slip as oil industry bounces back from Harvey(Adds Port Arthur, Eagle Ford updates)"
Exxon,2017-9,"NEW YORK, Sept 4 (Reuters) - U.S. gasoline prices fell on Monday as the nation's oil heartland continued to claw its way back from the devastation wrought by Storm Harvey, with shipping channels, pipelines and refineries restarting operations."
Exxon,2017-9,"Port operations across the U.S. Gulf Coast oil and gas hub were resuming, although many still had restrictions on vessel draft, according to U.S. Coast Guard updates."
Exxon,2017-9,Key fuel pipelines planned to restart as more of the oil refineries that feed them ramped up production.
Exxon,2017-9,"Benchmark U.S. gasoline futures fell by more than 3 percent, and retail prices edged up by only 1 cent a gallon on Monday, according to motorists advocacy group AAA, after climbing by more than 20 cents in the wake of Harvey, which was downgraded to a storm after making landfall as a hurricane."
Exxon,2017-9,"Harvey dumped as much as 50 inches (127 cm) of rain over Texas and Louisiana, forcing officials to close or restrict operations at ports from Corpus Christi, Texas, to Lake Charles, Louisiana. It also forced the closure of nearly a quarter of the nation's oil refining capacity."
Exxon,2017-9,"The U.S. Coast Guard on Monday allowed some barge traffic to enter Port Arthur, Texas, home of the country's largest oil refinery, and is considering allowing ships to enter on Tuesday, a spokesman said. [nL2N1LL0ZX]"
Exxon,2017-9,"Port Arthur was one of three Texas ports that was still closed, along with Beaumont and Port Orange. The state's 25 other ports were operational as of Monday, some with restrictions, according to Colonel Lars Zetterstrom, Galveston District commander of the U.S. Army Corps of Engineers."
Exxon,2017-9,"Alberto Hernandez, a watch supervisor at the U.S. Coast Guard, said on Monday that ships were exiting and entering the Houston Ship Channel, which links the Port of Houston, the busiest petrochemical port, to the Gulf of Mexico."
Exxon,2017-9,"The channel is open to just past Exxon Mobil Corp's Baytown refinery to vessels up to a 40-foot (12-meter) draft, while salvage efforts continued to remove a sunken drydock in an industrial portion, officials said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Hernandez said there was no time frame for removing the drydock debris from the main stem of the channel, which is key to moving crude oil to refineries."
Exxon,2017-9,Restarts of pipelines that move fuel from refineries to the rest of the nation also were alleviating worries about shortages.
Exxon,2017-9,"Colonial Pipeline Co , which transports more than 3 million barrels per day (bpd) of gasoline, diesel and jet fuel from Gulf Coast refineries to Northeastern markets, said the restart on Monday afternoon of its main distillate line between Houston and Hebert, Texas, would take ""a few hours."" It plans the same restart process for the gasoline line between those points on Tuesday. [nENN0OPWF2]"
Exxon,2017-9,The Explorer Pipeline planned to reopen its 24-inch (61 cm) Oklahoma-to-Midwest fuel pipeline on Monday after reopening its 28-inch (71 cm) Texas-to-Oklahoma line on Sunday. [L2N1LL01W]
Exxon,2017-9,"ExxonMobil said on Monday its pipeline division was initiating supply of gasoline and other fuels to the Houston area after making ""significant progress"" on restarting the lines."
Exxon,2017-9,"Fuels-producing refineries also were ramping up output. Valero Energy Corp was restarting multiple units at its 335,000 bpd Port Arthur, Texas, refinery on Monday, according to regulatory filings, and the company said its 293,000 bpd Corpus Christi and 225,000-bpd Texas City refineries were back to pre-storm levels of production.[nL2N1LL0UV][nL8N1LL3UW]"
Exxon,2017-9,"ExxonMobil's 560,500-bpd Baytown, Texas, refinery, the nation's second-largest, began restarting during the weekend, while Phillips 66 said it was resuming operations at its 247,000-bpd Sweeny refinery. [nL2N1LJ0FW]"
Exxon,2017-9,"Crude oil operations were also edging back to normal. ConocoPhillips said its oil production in the Eagle Ford shale region was expected to reach 80 percent of its pre-storm level of 130,000 barrels of oil equivalent per day by Monday evening, while the number of U.S. Gulf oil and gas production platforms with evacuated personnel after Hurricane Harvey dropped to 14, down from 30, according to the U.S. Bureau of Safety and Environmental Enforcement. [nL8N1LL41G]"
Exxon,2017-9,"Still, the bureau said the total of U.S. Gulf of Mexico oil production closed increased to roughly 6.94 percent, or 121,484 bpd, up from 5.5 percent on Sunday. It did not give a reason for the increase."

Exxon,2017-9,EXCLUSIVE-Indonesia's Pertamina receives first license to export gasoil -sources - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170904T114629.655+0000}}EXCLUSIVE-Indonesia's Pertamina receives first license to export gasoil -sources* Crowded retail market, lower domestic demand drives up inventory"
Exxon,2017-9,"SINGAPORE/JAKARTA, Sept 4 (Reuters) - Indonesia's Pertamina [PERTM.UL] has received a license from the government to export gasoil for the first time, three sources close to the matter said on Monday, although the state oil company is planning to prioritize domestic sales if possible."
Exxon,2017-9,"Pertamina is typically an importer of gasoil, as diesel is called in most Asian markets, but inbound shipments have declined over the years as it ramped up refining output and demand from the mining sector slowed."
Exxon,2017-9,"With other gasoil sellers - such as Royal Dutch Shell , Exxon Mobil Corp and Solaris Prima Energy - crowding into the retail market, and an increased biodiesel mandate in 2016 reducing conventional consumption, Pertamina's supply of the fuel has also outperformed demand, said Toharso, director of refineries at Pertamina, who goes by one name."
Exxon,2017-9,"If Pertamina exports its surplus fuel, it would help ease supply tightness in Asia caused by Tropical Storm Harvey, which drove up the Asian gasoil margins to a one-and-a-half month high, traders said. [nL4N1LG30C] [nL8N1LH44K]"
Exxon,2017-9,"The company, though, is also taking steps to sell more gasoil into its domestic market by asking the government to grant it a monopoly on diesel imports, which would force the other retailers to buy from Pertamina."
Exxon,2017-9,"The state oil company received the gasoil export license two to three weeks ago, and it is developing a standard operating procedure on how to export the cargoes, the sources said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Still, ""we will try our best to sell in the domestic market,"" Toto Nugroho, senior vice president at Pertamina for integrated supply chain, told Reuters."
Exxon,2017-9,"But if market competition means storage inventories build up, ""the last resort is to export,"" he said."
Exxon,2017-9,Pertamina declined to give details on possible export volumes or a timeline of shipments.
Exxon,2017-9,"Pertamina supplies about 70 percent of Indonesia's gasoil needs, while private firms supply the rest, Toharso said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Many of the private firms import their gasoil, but Pertamina is lobbying Jakarta to name it the country's exclusive importer of the fuel, a move that would alleviate the state oil company's surplus and possibly negate its need to export the fuel."
Exxon,2017-9,"""Pertamina is encouraging the Energy Ministry to make other companies not to import gasoil and just buy it from Pertamina,"" said Toharso."
Exxon,2017-9,Indonesia's Energy Ministry did not address a Reuters query asking if it will approve Pertamina's request.
Exxon,2017-9,"Dadan Kusdiana, a spokesman for the ministry said it will ""encourage (retail) companies to purchase from Pertamina first before they import."""
Exxon,2017-9,"""Pertamina has also sent an offer letter to other (retail) companies that need gasoil,"" Kusdiana said."
Exxon,2017-9,"But the prices offered by Pertamina are higher than buying from the international market, said a buyer who declined to be named as he was not authorised to speak with media."
Exxon,2017-9,"""We can easily absorb the cargoes as long as the price is competitive,"" the buyer said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Nearly two-thirds of Indonesia's gasoil is used in its transport sector for commercial vehicles, which is expected to grow at 3 to 5 percent this year. The rest is used in the country's industrial and mining sectors."
Exxon,2017-9,"Solaris Prima Energy is a subsidiary of China-owned trader Unipec Singapore, whose parent company is Asia's top refiner Sinopec Corp <600028.SS>."
Exxon,2017-9,RPT-Harvey's wake tempers bullish outlook for U.S. oil output growth - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170904T060001.760+0000}}RPT-Harvey's wake tempers bullish outlook for U.S. oil output growth(Repeats story originally published Sept 1, no changes)"
Exxon,2017-9,"HOUSTON, Sept 1 (Reuters) - Damage and delays from Tropical Storm Harvey will hold the U.S. oil industry back from achieving a targeted 10 million barrels per day of production anytime soon, according to analysts, a setback in America's fight for global market share with OPEC."
Exxon,2017-9,"The storm, which flooded refineries, wells and pipelines across Texas, added to a string of problems oil companies already faced, like low crude prices and expensive engineering challenges at new shale wells. [nL2N1LG1DG]"
Exxon,2017-9,"Earlier this year, oil analysts and some company executives had anticipated that the United States could top the 10 million bpd mark by year-end. That would have been a 14 percent increase, taking U.S. output to a level not seen since the 1970s."
Exxon,2017-9,"But then Harvey knocked out about a quarter of U.S. refining capacity and shuttered transport routes for crude, gasoline, diesel and other products. The storm's impacts sent gasoline prices soaring but also crimped demand for crude. [nL2N1LI0GW][nL2N1LH0T8]"
Exxon,2017-9,Bringing all that infrastructure back to normal operations could take weeks or months.
Exxon,2017-9,"""Harvey is going to have a longer effect on the oil industry than anyone would have imagined,"" said Dan Katzenberg, an oil industry analyst at R.W. Baird & Co. ""It's just a real mess on so many levels."""
Exxon,2017-9,"The Organization of the Petroleum Exporting Countries is frustrated that the storm has not pushed global prices higher, with one OPEC delegate telling Reuters, ""It seems no event will move the oil price up much.""[nL8N1LH4M4]"
Exxon,2017-9,"Slipping production after a major storm is not unprecedented: U.S. output slipped after Hurricane Dennis in 1999, Hurricane Ivan in 2004 and Hurricane Katrina in 2005, forcing a range of industry and government reactions."
Exxon,2017-9,"On Friday, U.S. Energy Secretary Rick Perry said he had authorized the release of 4.5 million barrels from the U.S. Strategic Petroleum Reserve. The move, aimed at helping a handful of Gulf Coast refiners deal with local supply disruptions, will likely depress oil prices further.[nL2N1LI1DA]"
Exxon,2017-9,"The Energy Information Administration (EIA) earlier this year had forecast that technological and process improvements would lift U.S. production sharply, leading some analysts and executives to predict 10 million bpd by December."
Exxon,2017-9,"But in recent months those expectations dimmed. Producers, showing signs of financial strain from the tepid oil prices, pared budgets for the year."
Exxon,2017-9,"Companies also face problems with pressure imbalance and high natural gas levels at new shale oil wells in the Permian Basin, the largest U.S. oilfield. [nL1N1KO0Z0]"
Exxon,2017-9,"The EIA on Thursday revised lower its data on U.S. oil production for June, saying it fell nearly 1 percent in the month to about 9.1 million bpd. Analysts called that a bad omen for the rest of the summer."
Exxon,2017-9,"Harvey forced Exxon Mobil Corp , Royal Dutch Shell PLC , Marathon Oil Corp , Statoil ASA and other producers in the Eagle Ford shale region of Texas and the U.S. Gulf of Mexico to halt production and the drilling and fracking of shale wells."
Exxon,2017-9,"More than a quarter of Gulf production went offline due to the storm, according to government data. In the Eagle Ford shale, producers on Friday were still assessing damage, but most saw operations slow or grind to a halt.[nL2N1LC0CG]"
Exxon,2017-9,"""At this point, we're really waiting to see what the cumulative effect will be"" from Harvey, said Paul Hesse of the U.S. Energy Information Administration."
Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon lost nearly 100,000 bpd of production, and Shell has so far lost more than 700,000 bpd."
Exxon,2017-9,"ConocoPhillips , meanwhile, said it does not plan to reopen its headquarters, which abuts a Houston reservoir that nearly breached, until Sept. 11."
Exxon,2017-9,"""That 10 million (bpd) level is just not going to happen in the next two years at least,"" said Anas Alhajji, an independent oil analyst and economist. ""The impact of Harvey adds to existing woes."""

Exxon,2017-9,UPDATE 3-U.S. gasoline prices slip as oil industry bounces back from Harvey - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170904T210245.168+0000}}UPDATE 3-U.S. gasoline prices slip as oil industry bounces back from Harvey(Adds Port Arthur, Eagle Ford updates)"
Exxon,2017-9,"NEW YORK, Sept 4 (Reuters) - U.S. gasoline prices fell on Monday as the nation's oil heartland continued to claw its way back from the devastation wrought by Storm Harvey, with shipping channels, pipelines and refineries restarting operations."
Exxon,2017-9,"Port operations across the U.S. Gulf Coast oil and gas hub were resuming, although many still had restrictions on vessel draft, according to U.S. Coast Guard updates."
Exxon,2017-9,Key fuel pipelines planned to restart as more of the oil refineries that feed them ramped up production.
Exxon,2017-9,"Benchmark U.S. gasoline futures fell by more than 3 percent, and retail prices edged up by only 1 cent a gallon on Monday, according to motorists advocacy group AAA, after climbing by more than 20 cents in the wake of Harvey, which was downgraded to a storm after making landfall as a hurricane."
Exxon,2017-9,"Harvey dumped as much as 50 inches (127 cm) of rain over Texas and Louisiana, forcing officials to close or restrict operations at ports from Corpus Christi, Texas, to Lake Charles, Louisiana. It also forced the closure of nearly a quarter of the nation's oil refining capacity."
Exxon,2017-9,"The U.S. Coast Guard on Monday allowed some barge traffic to enter Port Arthur, Texas, home of the country's largest oil refinery, and is considering allowing ships to enter on Tuesday, a spokesman said. [nL2N1LL0ZX]"
Exxon,2017-9,"Port Arthur was one of three Texas ports that was still closed, along with Beaumont and Port Orange. The state's 25 other ports were operational as of Monday, some with restrictions, according to Colonel Lars Zetterstrom, Galveston District commander of the U.S. Army Corps of Engineers."
Exxon,2017-9,"Alberto Hernandez, a watch supervisor at the U.S. Coast Guard, said on Monday that ships were exiting and entering the Houston Ship Channel, which links the Port of Houston, the busiest petrochemical port, to the Gulf of Mexico."
Exxon,2017-9,"The channel is open to just past Exxon Mobil Corp's Baytown refinery to vessels up to a 40-foot (12-meter) draft, while salvage efforts continued to remove a sunken drydock in an industrial portion, officials said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Hernandez said there was no time frame for removing the drydock debris from the main stem of the channel, which is key to moving crude oil to refineries."
Exxon,2017-9,Restarts of pipelines that move fuel from refineries to the rest of the nation also were alleviating worries about shortages.
Exxon,2017-9,"Colonial Pipeline Co , which transports more than 3 million barrels per day (bpd) of gasoline, diesel and jet fuel from Gulf Coast refineries to Northeastern markets, said the restart on Monday afternoon of its main distillate line between Houston and Hebert, Texas, would take ""a few hours."" It plans the same restart process for the gasoline line between those points on Tuesday. [nENN0OPWF2]"
Exxon,2017-9,The Explorer Pipeline planned to reopen its 24-inch (61 cm) Oklahoma-to-Midwest fuel pipeline on Monday after reopening its 28-inch (71 cm) Texas-to-Oklahoma line on Sunday. [L2N1LL01W]
Exxon,2017-9,"ExxonMobil said on Monday its pipeline division was initiating supply of gasoline and other fuels to the Houston area after making ""significant progress"" on restarting the lines."
Exxon,2017-9,"Fuels-producing refineries also were ramping up output. Valero Energy Corp was restarting multiple units at its 335,000 bpd Port Arthur, Texas, refinery on Monday, according to regulatory filings, and the company said its 293,000 bpd Corpus Christi and 225,000-bpd Texas City refineries were back to pre-storm levels of production.[nL2N1LL0UV][nL8N1LL3UW]"
Exxon,2017-9,"ExxonMobil's 560,500-bpd Baytown, Texas, refinery, the nation's second-largest, began restarting during the weekend, while Phillips 66 said it was resuming operations at its 247,000-bpd Sweeny refinery. [nL2N1LJ0FW]"
Exxon,2017-9,"Crude oil operations were also edging back to normal. ConocoPhillips said its oil production in the Eagle Ford shale region was expected to reach 80 percent of its pre-storm level of 130,000 barrels of oil equivalent per day by Monday evening, while the number of U.S. Gulf oil and gas production platforms with evacuated personnel after Hurricane Harvey dropped to 14, down from 30, according to the U.S. Bureau of Safety and Environmental Enforcement. [nL8N1LL41G]"
Exxon,2017-9,"Still, the bureau said the total of U.S. Gulf of Mexico oil production closed increased to roughly 6.94 percent, or 121,484 bpd, up from 5.5 percent on Sunday. It did not give a reason for the increase."

Exxon,2017-9,EXCLUSIVE-Indonesia's Pertamina receives first license to export gasoil -sources - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170904T114629.655+0000}}EXCLUSIVE-Indonesia's Pertamina receives first license to export gasoil -sources* Crowded retail market, lower domestic demand drives up inventory"
Exxon,2017-9,"SINGAPORE/JAKARTA, Sept 4 (Reuters) - Indonesia's Pertamina [PERTM.UL] has received a license from the government to export gasoil for the first time, three sources close to the matter said on Monday, although the state oil company is planning to prioritize domestic sales if possible."
Exxon,2017-9,"Pertamina is typically an importer of gasoil, as diesel is called in most Asian markets, but inbound shipments have declined over the years as it ramped up refining output and demand from the mining sector slowed."
Exxon,2017-9,"With other gasoil sellers - such as Royal Dutch Shell , Exxon Mobil Corp and Solaris Prima Energy - crowding into the retail market, and an increased biodiesel mandate in 2016 reducing conventional consumption, Pertamina's supply of the fuel has also outperformed demand, said Toharso, director of refineries at Pertamina, who goes by one name."
Exxon,2017-9,"If Pertamina exports its surplus fuel, it would help ease supply tightness in Asia caused by Tropical Storm Harvey, which drove up the Asian gasoil margins to a one-and-a-half month high, traders said. [nL4N1LG30C] [nL8N1LH44K]"
Exxon,2017-9,"The company, though, is also taking steps to sell more gasoil into its domestic market by asking the government to grant it a monopoly on diesel imports, which would force the other retailers to buy from Pertamina."
Exxon,2017-9,"The state oil company received the gasoil export license two to three weeks ago, and it is developing a standard operating procedure on how to export the cargoes, the sources said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Still, ""we will try our best to sell in the domestic market,"" Toto Nugroho, senior vice president at Pertamina for integrated supply chain, told Reuters."
Exxon,2017-9,"But if market competition means storage inventories build up, ""the last resort is to export,"" he said."
Exxon,2017-9,Pertamina declined to give details on possible export volumes or a timeline of shipments.
Exxon,2017-9,"Pertamina supplies about 70 percent of Indonesia's gasoil needs, while private firms supply the rest, Toharso said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Many of the private firms import their gasoil, but Pertamina is lobbying Jakarta to name it the country's exclusive importer of the fuel, a move that would alleviate the state oil company's surplus and possibly negate its need to export the fuel."
Exxon,2017-9,"""Pertamina is encouraging the Energy Ministry to make other companies not to import gasoil and just buy it from Pertamina,"" said Toharso."
Exxon,2017-9,Indonesia's Energy Ministry did not address a Reuters query asking if it will approve Pertamina's request.
Exxon,2017-9,"Dadan Kusdiana, a spokesman for the ministry said it will ""encourage (retail) companies to purchase from Pertamina first before they import."""
Exxon,2017-9,"""Pertamina has also sent an offer letter to other (retail) companies that need gasoil,"" Kusdiana said."
Exxon,2017-9,"But the prices offered by Pertamina are higher than buying from the international market, said a buyer who declined to be named as he was not authorised to speak with media."
Exxon,2017-9,"""We can easily absorb the cargoes as long as the price is competitive,"" the buyer said."
Exxon,2017-9,"Nearly two-thirds of Indonesia's gasoil is used in its transport sector for commercial vehicles, which is expected to grow at 3 to 5 percent this year. The rest is used in the country's industrial and mining sectors."
Exxon,2017-9,"Solaris Prima Energy is a subsidiary of China-owned trader Unipec Singapore, whose parent company is Asia's top refiner Sinopec Corp <600028.SS>."
Exxon,2017-9,RPT-Harvey's wake tempers bullish outlook for U.S. oil output growth - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,"{{20170904T060001.760+0000}}RPT-Harvey's wake tempers bullish outlook for U.S. oil output growth(Repeats story originally published Sept 1, no changes)"
Exxon,2017-9,"HOUSTON, Sept 1 (Reuters) - Damage and delays from Tropical Storm Harvey will hold the U.S. oil industry back from achieving a targeted 10 million barrels per day of production anytime soon, according to analysts, a setback in America's fight for global market share with OPEC."
Exxon,2017-9,"The storm, which flooded refineries, wells and pipelines across Texas, added to a string of problems oil companies already faced, like low crude prices and expensive engineering challenges at new shale wells. [nL2N1LG1DG]"
Exxon,2017-9,"Earlier this year, oil analysts and some company executives had anticipated that the United States could top the 10 million bpd mark by year-end. That would have been a 14 percent increase, taking U.S. output to a level not seen since the 1970s."
Exxon,2017-9,"But then Harvey knocked out about a quarter of U.S. refining capacity and shuttered transport routes for crude, gasoline, diesel and other products. The storm's impacts sent gasoline prices soaring but also crimped demand for crude. [nL2N1LI0GW][nL2N1LH0T8]"
Exxon,2017-9,Bringing all that infrastructure back to normal operations could take weeks or months.
Exxon,2017-9,"""Harvey is going to have a longer effect on the oil industry than anyone would have imagined,"" said Dan Katzenberg, an oil industry analyst at R.W. Baird & Co. ""It's just a real mess on so many levels."""
Exxon,2017-9,"The Organization of the Petroleum Exporting Countries is frustrated that the storm has not pushed global prices higher, with one OPEC delegate telling Reuters, ""It seems no event will move the oil price up much.""[nL8N1LH4M4]"
Exxon,2017-9,"Slipping production after a major storm is not unprecedented: U.S. output slipped after Hurricane Dennis in 1999, Hurricane Ivan in 2004 and Hurricane Katrina in 2005, forcing a range of industry and government reactions."
Exxon,2017-9,"On Friday, U.S. Energy Secretary Rick Perry said he had authorized the release of 4.5 million barrels from the U.S. Strategic Petroleum Reserve. The move, aimed at helping a handful of Gulf Coast refiners deal with local supply disruptions, will likely depress oil prices further.[nL2N1LI1DA]"
Exxon,2017-9,"The Energy Information Administration (EIA) earlier this year had forecast that technological and process improvements would lift U.S. production sharply, leading some analysts and executives to predict 10 million bpd by December."
Exxon,2017-9,"But in recent months those expectations dimmed. Producers, showing signs of financial strain from the tepid oil prices, pared budgets for the year."
Exxon,2017-9,"Companies also face problems with pressure imbalance and high natural gas levels at new shale oil wells in the Permian Basin, the largest U.S. oilfield. [nL1N1KO0Z0]"
Exxon,2017-9,"The EIA on Thursday revised lower its data on U.S. oil production for June, saying it fell nearly 1 percent in the month to about 9.1 million bpd. Analysts called that a bad omen for the rest of the summer."
Exxon,2017-9,"Harvey forced Exxon Mobil Corp , Royal Dutch Shell PLC , Marathon Oil Corp , Statoil ASA and other producers in the Eagle Ford shale region of Texas and the U.S. Gulf of Mexico to halt production and the drilling and fracking of shale wells."
Exxon,2017-9,"More than a quarter of Gulf production went offline due to the storm, according to government data. In the Eagle Ford shale, producers on Friday were still assessing damage, but most saw operations slow or grind to a halt.[nL2N1LC0CG]"
Exxon,2017-9,"""At this point, we're really waiting to see what the cumulative effect will be"" from Harvey, said Paul Hesse of the U.S. Energy Information Administration."
Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon lost nearly 100,000 bpd of production, and Shell has so far lost more than 700,000 bpd."
Exxon,2017-9,"ConocoPhillips , meanwhile, said it does not plan to reopen its headquarters, which abuts a Houston reservoir that nearly breached, until Sept. 11."
Exxon,2017-9,"""That 10 million (bpd) level is just not going to happen in the next two years at least,"" said Anas Alhajji, an independent oil analyst and economist. ""The impact of Harvey adds to existing woes."""

Exxon,2017-9,"The Organization of the Petroleum Exporting Countries is frustrated that the storm has not pushed global prices higher, with one OPEC delegate telling Reuters, ""It seems no event will move the oil price up much.""[nL8N1LH4M4]"
Exxon,2017-9,"Slipping production after a major storm is not unprecedented: U.S. output slipped after Hurricane Dennis in 1999, Hurricane Ivan in 2004 and Hurricane Katrina in 2005, forcing a range of industry and government reactions."
Exxon,2017-9,"On Friday, U.S. Energy Secretary Rick Perry said he had authorized the release of 4.5 million barrels from the U.S. Strategic Petroleum Reserve. The move, aimed at helping a handful of Gulf Coast refiners deal with local supply disruptions, will likely depress oil prices further.[nL2N1LI1DA]"
Exxon,2017-9,"The Energy Information Administration (EIA) earlier this year had forecast that technological and process improvements would lift U.S. production sharply, leading some analysts and executives to predict 10 million bpd by December."
Exxon,2017-9,"But in recent months those expectations dimmed. Producers, showing signs of financial strain from the tepid oil prices, pared budgets for the year."
Exxon,2017-9,"Companies also face problems with pressure imbalance and high natural gas levels at new shale oil wells in the Permian Basin, the largest U.S. oilfield. [nL1N1KO0Z0]"
Exxon,2017-9,"The EIA on Thursday revised lower its data on U.S. oil production for June, saying it fell nearly 1 percent in the month to about 9.1 million bpd. Analysts called that a bad omen for the rest of the summer."
Exxon,2017-9,"Harvey forced Exxon Mobil Corp , Royal Dutch Shell PLC , Marathon Oil Corp , Statoil ASA and other producers in the Eagle Ford shale region of Texas and the U.S. Gulf of Mexico to halt production and the drilling and fracking of shale wells."
Exxon,2017-9,"More than a quarter of Gulf production went offline due to the storm, according to government data. In the Eagle Ford shale, producers on Friday were still assessing damage, but most saw operations slow or grind to a halt.[nL2N1LC0CG]"
Exxon,2017-9,"""At this point, we're really waiting to see what the cumulative effect will be"" from Harvey, said Paul Hesse of the U.S. Energy Information Administration."
Exxon,2017-9,"Exxon lost nearly 100,000 bpd of production, and Shell has so far lost more than 700,000 bpd."
Exxon,2017-9,"ConocoPhillips , meanwhile, said it does not plan to reopen its headquarters, which abuts a Houston reservoir that nearly breached, until Sept. 11."
Exxon,2017-9,"""That 10 million (bpd) level is just not going to happen in the next two years at least,"" said Anas Alhajji, an independent oil analyst and economist. ""The impact of Harvey adds to existing woes."""

Exxon,2017-9,"NEW YORK, Sept 1 (Reuters Breakingviews) - Activist hedge-fund manager Paul Singer recently warned that the rise of so-called passive investing risked distorting markets and ""devouring capitalism."" But although index-tracking funds can't sell stocks when they spot trouble ahead, that doesn't mean they are without influence."
Exxon,2017-9,"In an open letter to corporate directors, Vanguard Chairman and Chief Executive William McNabb said the firm was determined to press its investors' interest and prod companies to manage for the long term precisely because the index funds that comprise nearly three-quarters of its assets hold their securities almost indefinitely. Among other things, he stressed the need for gender diversity on boards, an issue rival indexing heavyweight State Street Global Advisors championed this year too."

Exxon,2017-9,Future of oil takes centre stage in Norwegian election - Reuters News
Exxon,2017-9,{{20170831T140002.879+0000}}Future of oil takes centre stage in Norwegian election* Ruling Conservatives pitted against opposition Labour
Exxon,2017-9,* Race is too close to call ahead of Sept. 11 election
Exxon,2017-9,"STAVANGER, Norway, Aug 31 (Reuters) - The future of Norway's oil sector is emerging as a key issue for voters in a Sept. 11 parliamentary election, nowhere more so than in the oil capital of Stavanger."
Exxon,2017-9,The right-wing bloc of Conservative Prime Minister Erna Solberg is neck-and-neck in opinion polls with an opposition grouping led by Jonas Gahr Stoere's Labour.
Exxon,2017-9,"Should neither secure a majority, the smaller Green party - which pledges to stop oil exploration and phase out production within 15 years - could become kingmakers."
Exxon,2017-9,"There is little chance of the Greens being able to call time on Norway's number one industry, which all major parties back to the hilt, accounts for half of national exports and employs over 180,000 people."
Exxon,2017-9,"But they have been gradually gathering support over the past four years and are polling at about 5 percent of the vote, underlining changes in Norwegian society and divisions over the future of oil."
Exxon,2017-9,"Should they hold the balance of power, they could seek to force compromises to trim the oil industry's ambitions, with environmentalists in recent months focusing on the need to limit oil companies' expansion in the Arctic."
Exxon,2017-9,"The Norwegian oil sector is still in recovery mode after thousands of local jobs were lost when crude prices crashed between 2014 and 2016. So the risk of any curbing of its prospects is high in people's minds in Stavanger, a windswept west coast city set among fjords."
Exxon,2017-9,"""If you were to just close down this industry, what are we supposed to live off? This is a big question for many,"" said Egil Ellingsen, 38, a Lutheran pastor who said he had counselled many people in the area who had lost their jobs."
Exxon,2017-9,"Ellingsen organised a public debate at his church last weekend with local parliamentary candidates, attended by about 800 people."
Exxon,2017-9,"The subject of jobs - how to create them, how people would survive if the oil industry declined - surfaced regularly during the debate."
Exxon,2017-9,"At one point Ellingsen asked the local Green candidate: ""Can you give me concrete examples of what jobs people could do if oil stops?"""
Exxon,2017-9,The candidate cited the offshore wind industry and the forestry and fisheries sectors as examples.
Exxon,2017-9,"Such assurances are not assuaging the concerns of workers at Dusavik port, outside Stavanger, which Total , ExxonMobil and Statoil use to ship equipment to their platforms in the North Sea."
Exxon,2017-9,"On a cloudy morning, staff are unloading drilling fluid from the Normand Leader ship just back from the Johan Sverdrup oil and gas field, which Norwegian state-controlled Statoil and its partners are developing offshore."
Exxon,2017-9,Production at the giant field - up to 3.3 billion barrels of oil - is due to start in 2019 but it is already keeping the harbour busy.
Exxon,2017-9,"After Johan Sverdrup was discovered in 2010, the port's operator, NorSea Group, invested 220 million crowns ($28.53 million) in its infrastructure to accommodate increased activity."
Exxon,2017-9,"Even as crude prices plunged, it kept all its 150 full-time employees at Dusavik, but let go the 20-30 workers who were on temporary contracts at Dusavik and its sister port in nearby Tananger."
Exxon,2017-9,"Rune Veenstra, the port's managing director, said the election campaign was sending out conflicting signals and creating uncertainty. What his company needed more than anything was clarity and predictability so that it can make long-term investments, he added."
Exxon,2017-9,"""If we can't have a clear direction, it is no good for anyone,"" Veenstra told Reuters."
Exxon,2017-9,"The main parties say they will not give ground to the Greens or any other group seeking to curb Norway's oil sector, which is pivotal to a national economy that is turning a corner after a couple of slow years."
Exxon,2017-9,"In the first half of 2017, the economy grew more than expected and reached 0.7 percent in the second quarter, data from Statistics Norway showed on Aug. 24. [nL8N1LA0WJ]"
Exxon,2017-9,"The current government coalition, the centre-right Conservatives and the populist Progress Party, claim credit for the turnaround. Their approach has been to cut taxes on businesses and individuals and plug the gap thanks to Norway's near-$1 trillion sovereign wealth fund."
Exxon,2017-9,"""This is a sign that the economic policy that the government has been running over the last years has been (right),"" Health Minister Bent Hoeie, a Conservative, told Reuters."
Exxon,2017-9,"That view is shared among some voters, such as 47-year-old Finn, a former oil worker who says he will vote for the Conservatives."
Exxon,2017-9,"""I am interested in schools and creating workplace opportunities ... the Conservatives have a better programme,"" he said. He declined to give his full name."
Exxon,2017-9,"But Labour, which was in government in 2005-2013, is emphasising that, even though the economy is on the up, there are still challenges to address if the country wants to finance its cradle-to-grave welfare state in the future."
Exxon,2017-9,"""We have to make sure that more of those who are outside (the job market) get an opportunity to have a job in the future,"" Hadia Tajik, Labour's deputy leader, told Reuters."
Exxon,2017-9,"Many Labour supporters told Reuters they would vote for the party because it was best at delivering good public services, such as schools and hospitals."
Exxon,2017-9,"""When Labour was in power, the schools, the hospitals, everything was good. Now it is not,"" said Atif Nisar, a 39-year-old taxi driver. ""My whole family has decided, we are all voting Labour."""
